# Portaconv → portagenty integration handoff

_Captured via `pconv dump --latest --workspace-toml auto` from
portaconv's current session on 2026-04-21. Use this as starting context
for a fresh Claude session in the **portagenty** workspace._

## Scope

This is the full transcript of the session in which portaconv was built
up from bootstrap to feature-complete for v0.1, then pivoted to **how
portagenty should integrate with portaconv** in the last ~150 messages.

The portagenty-side actionable items are:

1. **`pa init --with-agent-hooks` flag** — scaffolds `.mcp.json`,
   `.claude/commands/` (slash commands that shell out to pconv), and
   `.claude/skills/` (capability manifest so Claude Code agents
   self-discover pconv). Optional flag; skips if pconv isn't on PATH.
2. **`pa convos` subcommand** — small shim that wraps `pconv` with
   workspace-toml context pre-filled. `pa convos list`,
   `pa convos last`, `pa convos dump <id>`.
3. **Auto-append `previous_paths` to workspace TOML on re-register** —
   when pa's auto-re-register-on-walk-up fires on a moved workspace,
   append the old cwd. Portaconv **already reads** this field (no pconv
   version bump required when pa starts writing it).

Search for '`pa init --with-agent-hooks`', '`pa convos`', or
'`previous_paths`' to jump to the relevant design discussions.

## Status on the portaconv side (already shipped)

- Core model + Claude Code adapter + markdown renderer + path rewrite
- `--workspace-toml <path|auto>` on list and dump
- `--latest` shortcut on dump for the one-command flow
- `--tail N` length control, `--since/--sort/--limit/--grep` on list
- Full MCP schema parity (all CLI flags mirrored)
- `previous_paths` read (defensive — bridges moved workspaces the
  moment pa starts writing)

## Note on redactions in this transcript

Personal/client project names have been sed-redacted to `<proj-X>` /
`<client-a>` placeholders throughout. The design discussion shape is
preserved; only the identifiers are scrubbed. The original scan +
redaction decision is itself captured near the end of the transcript
(grep for 'PII').

---

## Assistant

**tool call:** `Write`

```json
{
  "content": "# Phase 1 — Claude Code JSONL research spike\n\n## Context\n\nThe approved plan (`~/.claude/plans/piped-sauteeing-breeze.md`) gates\nPhase 2 (core model + adapter + CLI) on a research spike: read real\nClaude Code JSONLs, enumerate every record `type`, and decide which\nrecords map to the v0.1 `Conversation` schema vs. metadata-in-extensions\nvs. ignorable. The point is to avoid freezing types before the format\nhas been observed — per the user's resilience principle, we don't want\nadapter rewrites every time Claude Code's on-disk shape shifts.\n\nThe spike is the **only** work gated before types are committed.\nDeliverable is a single doc — `docs/adapter-notes-claude-code.md` —\nthat freezes the v0.1 contract for the Claude adapter. No production\ncode yet. The throwaway parser is a cargo example and gets deleted\nafter Phase 2 starts.\n\n**Local corpus**: 2607 JSONLs under `~/.claude/projects/`. Size spread\nranges from 115 B to 2 GB. Notable shape found during scan: many\nprojects contain a `subagents/` subdirectory with per-subagent JSONLs\n(e.g. `<project>/<parent-uuid>/subagents/agent-<hash>.jsonl`). The\napproved plan didn't call this out — the spike must decide whether\nv0.1 surfaces subagent sessions, hides them, or attaches them to their\nparent.\n\n## Approach\n\n### 1. Pick a representative sample (5 files)\n\nPull directly from `~/.claude/projects/`. Spread across size, encoding,\nand shape so the spike catches variety, not one JSONL's local habits.\n\n| Slot | Selection criterion | Purpose |\n|---|---|---|\n| **Tiny** | smallest JSONL > 0 B with ≥ 3 messages | Fast iteration; one-of-each record types |\n| **Small** | ~100 KB, WSL-encoded dir (`-mnt-c-…`) | Normal human session, WSL paths baked in |\n| **Medium** | 1–5 MB, Windows-encoded dir (`C--…`) | Confirms both encodings parse identically, exposes Windows paths in content |\n| **Subagent** | `…/subagents/agent-*.jsonl` | The undocumented shape — must be understood |\n| **Large** | ≥ 50 MB (avoid the 2 GB monster for iteration speed) | Validates streaming-line parse scales; surfaces rare record types |\n\nRecord each file's absolute path, size, line count, and encoded-dir\nname in the notes doc (redact the actual session UUIDs in public\ncommits if needed).\n\n### 2. Enumerate record types\n\nWalk each sample line-by-line. For every distinct JSON record, capture:\n\n- Top-level `type` value (e.g. `user`, `assistant`, `system`,\n  `file-history-snapshot`, `summary`, `tool_use`, …)\n- All top-level fields that appear for that type\n- Whether the record carries a nested `message.content` array (event\n  stream shape) or is a flat metadata record\n- For message records: the roles seen, the content-block variants\n  seen (`text`, `tool_use`, `tool_result`, `thinking`, `image`, …)\n- Whether `parentUuid` / `sessionId` / `cwd` / `gitBranch` / `version`\n  appear consistently\n\nResult lands in a table in `docs/adapter-notes-claude-code.md` with\none row per record type.\n\n### 3. Classify each record\n\nThree buckets, stated explicitly per record type:\n\n| Bucket | Meaning | v0.1 behavior |\n|---|---|---|\n| **Schema** | Maps to a `ContentBlock` in `Conversation.messages` | Normalized into the model |\n| **Extensions** | Conversation-level or message-level metadata worth preserving | Goes into `extensions: serde_json::Value` verbatim |\n| **Skip** | Known ignorable for v0.1 (e.g. internal caching noise) | Dropped with a one-line rationale |\n\nIf any record is unclassifiable, that's a flag to surface back to the\nuser before Phase 2 starts — don't guess.\n\nSubagent JSONLs specifically: decide **one** of\n- (a) v0.1 ignores them and lists only top-level session JSONLs, or\n- (b) v0.1 lists them with a `subagent_of: <parent-uuid>` field in\n  extensions,\n- (c) v0.1 merges them into the parent session's message stream.\n\nDefault recommendation: **(a)** — minimum surface, defer the nesting\nquestion until the adapter is real. But state the tradeoff in the\nnotes doc.\n\n### 4. Throwaway parser — prove the shape\n\nA single-file cargo example at `examples/scan-claude-jsonl.rs`\n(deleted before Phase 2 lands; not shipped in the crate).\n\nBehavior:\n- `cargo run --example scan-claude-jsonl -- <path-to-jsonl>`\n- Reads line-by-line (`BufRead::lines`, not slurp — the 50 MB sample\n  must not blow the heap)\n- For each line: parse as `serde_json::Value`, classify by top-level\n  `type`\n- Prints per-file summary:\n  `(total_records, by_type_counts, role_counts, tool_use_count,\n  tool_result_count, distinct_session_uuids)`\n- Uses only deps already in `Cargo.toml` (`serde_json`, `anyhow`)\n\nThis is the sanity check that the mental model from step 2 matches the\nbytes on disk. If counts come out wrong, the notes doc was wrong.\n\n### 5. Write `docs/adapter-notes-claude-code.md`\n\nThe only durable artifact. Contents:\n\n1. **Scope** — \"this doc freezes what the Claude Code adapter handles\n   in v0.1. Enumerate record types\n\nWalk each sample line-by-line. For every distinct JSON record, capture:\n\n- Top-level `type` value (e.g. `user`, `assistant`, `system`,\n  `file-history-snapshot`, `summary`, `tool_use`, …)\n- All top-level fields that appear for that type\n- Whether the record carries a nested `message.content` array (event\n  stream shape) or is a flat metadata record\n- For message records: the roles seen, the content-block variants\n  seen (`text`, `tool_use`, `tool_result`, `thinking`, `image`, …)\n- Whether `parentUuid` / `sessionId` / `cwd` / `gitBranch` / `version`\n  appear consistently\n\nResult lands in a table in `docs/adapter-notes-claude-code.md` with\none row per record type.\n\n### 3. Classify each record\n\nThree buckets, stated explicitly per record type:\n\n| Bucket | Meaning | v0.1 behavior |\n|---|---|---|\n| **Schema** | Maps to a `ContentBlock` in `Conversation.messages` | Normalized into the model |\n| **Extensions** | Conversation-level or message-level metadata worth preserving | Goes into `extensions: serde_json::Value` verbatim |\n| **Skip** | Known ignorable for v0.1 (e.g. internal caching noise) | Dropped with a one-line rationale |\n\nIf any record is unclassifiable, that's a flag to surface back to the\nuser before Phase 2 starts — don't guess.\n\nSubagent JSONLs specifically: decide **one** of\n- (a) v0.1 ignores them and lists only top-level session JSONLs, or\n- (b) v0.1 lists them with a `subagent_of: <parent-uuid>` field in\n  extensions,\n- (c) v0.1 merges them into the parent session's message stream.\n\nDefault recommendation: **(a)** — minimum surface, defer the nesting\nquestion until the adapter is real. Throwaway parser — prove the shape\n\nA single-file cargo example at `examples/scan-claude-jsonl.rs`\n(deleted before Phase 2 lands; not shipped in the crate).\n\nBehavior:\n- `cargo run --example scan-claude-jsonl -- <path-to-jsonl>`\n- Reads line-by-line (`BufRead::lines`, not slurp — the 50 MB sample\n  must not blow the heap)\n- For each line: parse as `serde_json::Value`, classify by top-level\n  `type`\n- Prints per-file summary:\n  `(total_records, by_type_counts, role_counts, tool_use_count,\n  tool_result_count, distinct_session_uuids)`\n- Uses only deps already in `Cargo.toml` (`serde_json`, `anyhow`)\n\nThis is the sanity check that the mental model from step 2 matches the\nbytes on disk. ## Assistant

**tool call:** `Write`

```json
{
  "content": "// Throwaway spike: enumerate record types in a Claude Code JSONL.\n// Deleted before Phase 2 ships — it exists only to validate the mental\n// model in docs/adapter-notes-claude-code.md against real bytes on disk.\n//\n// Usage: cargo run --example scan-claude-jsonl -- <path-to-jsonl> [more...]\n//\n// Streams line-by-line so a 50 MB session doesn't blow the heap. Per file:\n//   - total records, parse errors\n//   - top-level `type` → count\n//   - message roles → count\n//   - content-block variants → count\n//   - distinct sessionIds, cwds, gitBranches, versions\n//   - presence counts for parentUuid, uuid, timestamp\n//   - path-content probe: /mnt/ and drive-letter occurrences in content\n//\n// Uses only deps already in Cargo.toml (serde_json, anyhow).\n\nuse std::collections::BTreeMap;\nuse std::env;\nuse std::fs::File;\nuse std::io::{BufRead, BufReader};\nuse std::path::Path;\n\nuse anyhow::{Context, Result};\nuse serde_json::Value;\n\n#[derive(Default)]\nstruct Stats {\n    total: usize,\n    parse_errors: usize,\n    by_type: BTreeMap<String, usize>,\n    by_role: BTreeMap<String, usize>,\n    by_block: BTreeMap<String, usize>,\n    session_ids: BTreeMap<String, usize>,\n    cwds: BTreeMap<String, usize>,\n    git_branches: BTreeMap<String, usize>,\n    versions: BTreeMap<String, usize>,\n    has_parent_uuid: usize,\n    has_uuid: usize,\n    has_timestamp: usize,\n    wsl_path_hits: usize,     // \"/mnt/\" substring in content text\n    windows_path_hits: usize, // drive-letter form (e.g. \"C:\\\\\")\n    top_level_fields: BTreeMap<String, usize>,\n    unknown_block_samples: Vec<String>,\n}\n\nfn main() -> Result<()> {\n    let args: Vec<String> = env::args().skip(1).collect();\n    if args.is_empty() {\n        eprintln!(\"usage: scan-claude-jsonl <path> [more...]\");\n        std::process::exit(2);\n    }\n    for p in &args {\n        match scan_one(Path::new(p)) {\n            Ok(stats) => print_report(p, &stats),\n            Err(e) => eprintln!(\"ERROR scanning {p}: {e:#}\"),\n        }\n    }\n    Ok(())\n}\n\nfn scan_one(path: &Path) -> Result<Stats> {\n    let f = File::open(path).with_context(|| format!(\"open {}\", path.display()))?;\n    let rdr = BufReader::new(f);\n    let mut s = Stats::default();\n    for line in rdr.lines() {\n        let line = line?;\n        if line.trim().is_empty() {\n            continue;\n        }\n        s.total += 1;\n        let v: Value = match serde_json::from_str(&line) {\n            Ok(v) => v,\n            Err(_) => {\n                s.parse_errors += 1;\n                continue;\n            }\n        };\n\n        if let Some(obj) = v.as_object() {\n            for k in obj.keys() {\n                *s.top_level_fields.entry(k.clone()).or_default() += 1;\n            }\n        }\n\n        let ty = v\n            .get(\"type\")\n            .and_then(|x| x.as_str())\n            .unwrap_or(\"<no-type>\")\n            .to_string();\n        *s.by_type.entry(ty.clone()).or_default() += 1;\n\n        for (field, bucket) in [\n            (\"sessionId\", &mut s.session_ids),\n            (\"cwd\", &mut s.cwds),\n            (\"gitBranch\", &mut s.git_branches),\n            (\"version\", &mut s.versions),\n        ] {\n            if let Some(val) = v.get(field).and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {\n                *bucket.entry(val.to_string()).or_default() += 1;\n            }\n        }\n        if v.get(\"parentUuid\").is_some() {\n            s.has_parent_uuid += 1;\n        }\n        if v.get(\"uuid\").is_some() {\n            s.has_uuid += 1;\n        }\n        if v.get(\"timestamp\").is_some() {\n            s.has_timestamp += 1;\n        }\n\n        // The event-stream assumption: message-like records nest\n        // {role, content[]} under \"message\". Verify by walking it.\n        if let Some(msg) = v.get(\"message\") {\n            if let Some(role) = msg.get(\"role\").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {\n                *s.by_role.entry(role.to_string()).or_default() += 1;\n            }\n            walk_content(msg.get(\"content\"), &mut s);\n        } else if matches!(ty.as_str(), \"user\" | \"assistant\" | \"system\") {\n            // Some records may flatten role to top level — record that shape.\n            if let Some(role) = v.get(\"role\").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {\n                *s.by_role.entry(format!(\"flat:{role}\")).or_default() += 1;\n            }\n            walk_content(v.get(\"content\"), &mut s);\n        }\n\n        // Cheap path probe over the whole raw line — good enough to\n        // feed the path-rewrite design, not a true substring-in-content\n        // measurement. The notes doc must state this caveat.\n        if line.contains(\"/mnt/\") {\n            s.wsl_path_hits += 1;\n        }\n        if contains_drive_letter(&line) {\n            s.windows_path_hits += 1;\n        }\n    }\n    Ok(s)\n}\n\nfn walk_content(content: Option<&Value>, s: &mut Stats) {\n    let Some(c) = content else {\n        *s.by_block.entry(\"<no-content>\".into()).or_default() += 1;\n        return;\n    };\n    match c {\n        Value::String(_) => {\n            *s.by_block.entry(\"string\".into()).or_default() += 1;\n        }\n        Value::Array(arr) => {\n            for b in arr {\n                let bty = b\n                    .get(\"type\")\n                    .and_then(|x| x.as_str())\n                    .unwrap_or(\"<untyped>\")\n                    .to_string();\n                *s.by_block.entry(bty.clone()).or_default() += 1;\n                if matches!(\n                    bty.as_str(),\n                    \"text\" | \"tool_use\" | \"tool_result\" | \"thinking\" | \"image\"\n                ) {\n                    // known variants — nothing to record\n                } else if s.unknown_block_samples.len() < 3 {\n                    s.unknown_block_samples.push(bty);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        _ => {\n            *s.by_block.entry(\"<non-string-non-array>\".into()).or_default() += 1;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn contains_drive_letter(haystack: &str) -> bool {\n    // Crude: any `<letter>:\\\\` or `<letter>:/` sequence in the JSON-escaped\n    // stream. Matches the 72 C:\\ hits claim in the research doc.\n    let bytes = haystack.as_bytes();\n    for i in 0..bytes.len().saturating_sub(3) {\n        let a = bytes[i];\n        let b = bytes.get(i + 1);\n        let c = bytes.get(i + 2);\n        let d = bytes.get(i + 3);\n        let is_letter = a.is_ascii_alphabetic();\n        let colon = b == Some(&b':');\n        // \"X:\\\\\" appears as X:\\\\ in JSON source (two backslashes)\n        let esc_backslash = c == Some(&b'\\\\') && d == Some(&b'\\\\');\n        let fwd_slash = c == Some(&b'/');\n        if is_letter && colon && (esc_backslash || fwd_slash) {\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n    false\n}\n\nfn print_report(path: &str, s: &Stats) {\n    println!(\"=== {path} ===\");\n    println!(\"  total records        : {}\", s.total);\n    println!(\"  parse errors         : {}\", s.parse_errors);\n    println!(\"  has parentUuid       : {}\", s.has_parent_uuid);\n    println!(\"  has uuid             : {}\", s.has_uuid);\n    println!(\"  has timestamp        : {}\", s.has_timestamp);\n    println!(\"  WSL-path hit lines   : {}\", s.wsl_path_hits);\n    println!(\"  Windows-path hit lines: {}\", s.windows_path_hits);\n    println!(\"  top-level `type` counts:\");\n    for (k, v) in &s.by_type {\n        println!(\"    {k:30} {v}\");\n    }\n    println!(\"  roles seen:\");\n    for (k, v) in &s.by_role {\n        println!(\"    {k:30} {v}\");\n    }\n    println!(\"  content-block variants:\");\n    for (k, v) in &s.by_block {\n        println!(\"    {k:30} {v}\");\n    }\n    println!(\"  distinct sessionIds  : {}\", s.session_ids.len());\n    println!(\"  distinct cwds        : {}\", s.cwds.len());\n    if s.cwds.len() <= 4 {\n        for k in s.cwds.keys() {\n            println!(\"    cwd: {k}\");\n        }\n    }\n    println!(\"  distinct gitBranches : {}\", s.git_branches.len());\n    if s.git_branches.len() <= 4 {\n        for k in s.git_branches.keys() {\n            println!(\"    branch: {k}\");\n        }\n    }\n    println!(\"  distinct versions    : {}\", s.versions.len());\n    for k in s.versions.keys() {\n        println!(\"    version: {k}\");\n    }\n    if !s.unknown_block_samples.is_empty() {\n        println!(\"  UNKNOWN block types sampled:\");\n        for k in &s.unknown_block_samples {\n            println!(\"    {k}\");\n        }\n    }\n    println!(\"  top-level fields seen (field → record count):\");\n    for (k, v) in &s.top_level_fields {\n        println!(\"    {k:30} {v}\");\n    }\n    println!();\n}\n",
  "file_path": "/mnt/c/Users/Cybersader/Documents/1 Projects, Workspaces/portaconv/examples/scan-claude-jsonl.rs"
}
```

## Assistant

## Assistant

Rich dataset. Findings I'll bake into the notes:
- **6 record types** total: `user`, `assistant`, `system`, `file-history-snapshot`, `progress`, `queue-operation`
- **`agentId` field** identifies both subagent shapes (top-level `agent-*.jsonl` = older Claude version; `subagents/agent-*.jsonl` = newer) — same thing, two locations
- **Single JSONL can contain multiple sessionIds** (the 20MB sample had 2) — adapter must filter by sessionId, not assume file=session
- **Content path-poisoning confirmed at scale**: Windows-encoded dir has 464/489 lines referencing `/mnt/`
- **Compact-history**: `isCompactSummary`, `compactMetadata`, `logicalParentUuid` appear in long sessions
- **Content blocks seen**: `text`, `tool_use`, `tool_result`, `thinking` (no `image` in samples)
- Run took 5.5s across all 6 files (~22MB total) — streaming works

## Assistant

**tool call:** `Write`

```json
{
  "content": "# Claude Code adapter notes (v0.1)\n\nEmpirical freeze of what the Claude Code adapter handles in portaconv\nv0.1, based on a spike against six real JSONLs pulled from\n`~/.claude/projects/` on 2026-04-20 (host: Linux/WSL, Claude Code\nversions 2.0.76 → 2.1.51 observed).\n\nThis doc is the output of Phase 1 of the approved plan\n(`~/.claude/plans/piped-sauteeing-breeze.md`). The adapter trait and\nschema types get committed in Phase 2 against this contract.\n\n## 1. Scope\n\n- Normative: any record type listed in §3 is handled as specified.\n- Any record type not listed is **unknown** — the adapter must not\n  silently drop it; it must either land in a per-record\n  `extensions: serde_json::Value` bag or flip a one-line warning.\n- Schema contract itself (`Conversation` / `Message` / `ContentBlock`)\n  is locked in `knowledgebase/03-design-decisions.md`; this doc does\n  not reopen it. It only defines the adapter's mapping onto it.\n\n## 2. Sample inventory\n\nSix JSONLs, spread across size, OS encoding, and on-disk shape.\nParser: `examples/scan-claude-jsonl.rs` (throwaway, deleted before\nPhase 2 lands). Full output: `/tmp/pconv_scan_output.txt`.\n\n| # | Slot | Size | Lines | Encoded dir (prefix) | Filename shape | Claude ver(s) |\n|---|------|-----:|------:|---------------------|----------------|---------------|\n| 1 | Tiny | 708 B | 3 | `-mnt-c-…-<proj-f>` | `<uuid>.jsonl` | (no version field in records) |\n| 2 | Small WSL | 100 KB | 42 | `-mnt-c-…-<proj-b>` | `<uuid>.jsonl` | 2.1.39, 2.1.42 |\n| 3 | Medium Win | 995 KB | 489 | `C--…-<proj-d>` | `<uuid>.jsonl` | 2.1.20 |\n| 4 | Subagent (new) | 11 KB | 6 | `-mnt-c-…-<proj-e>/<parent-uuid>/subagents/` | `agent-acompact-<hash>.jsonl` | 2.1.51 |\n| 5 | Large | 19.8 MB | 805 | `-mnt-c-…-<proj-c>` | `<uuid>.jsonl` | 2.1.2, 2.1.9 |\n| 6 | Agent (old) | 80 KB | 23 | `-mnt-c-…-<client-a-project>` | `agent-<hash>.jsonl` | 2.0.76 |\n\nStreaming line-parse completed all six (≈22 MB combined) in **5.5 s\nwall-time** — well under the \"seconds not minutes\" bar the plan set.\nZero parse errors across 1368 records.\n\n## 3. Record type table\n\nThe top-level `type` discriminator has six values in this sample.\n\n| `type` | Description | Bucket | v0.1 handling | Notes |\n|---|---|---|---|---|\n| `user` | Conversational message, user role. `message.{role, content[]}` is the event-stream shape. | **Schema** | Map to `Message { role: User, content: Vec<ContentBlock>, timestamp, extensions }`. Copy top-level `uuid`, `parentUuid`, `requestId`, `isSidechain`, `slug`, `userType` into `message.extensions`. | Includes compact-summary records (`isCompactSummary: true`) — those are regular `user` records whose content is the summary text. Keep them. |\n| `assistant` | Conversational message, assistant role. Same event-stream shape. | **Schema** | Same as `user`. Content includes `tool_use` and `thinking` blocks alongside `text`. | `thinkingMetadata` on the record goes into `message.extensions`. |\n| `system` | Metadata event (e.g. `subtype: \"turn_duration\"` with `durationMs`). No `message.content`. | **Extensions** (conv-level) | Append as-is to `Conversation.extensions.system_events[]` (append-only array). Do not render to paste output in v0.1. | Only 6–9 per long session. Small. |\n| `file-history-snapshot` | Claude Code's file-tracking metadata: `{messageId, snapshot: {trackedFileBackups, timestamp}, isSnapshotUpdate}`. | **Skip** | Drop. Not surfaced in `Conversation.extensions`. | These files are tracked elsewhere in Claude's workspace; portaconv is not a file-state tool. |\n| `progress` | Live streaming events for subagent runs. Carries `data.{message, type: \"agent_progress\", prompt, agentId}` + `toolUseID` + `parentToolUseID`. | **Skip** | Drop. | The final assistant message already carries the consolidated `tool_use`; the stream is transient. Re-evaluate if v0.1 paste output looks lossy on subagent-heavy sessions. |\n| `queue-operation` | Claude Code's prompt-queue bookkeeping (`operation: \"enqueue\"`, raw user-typed `content`). | **Skip** | Drop. | Internal scheduling state; not part of the rendered dialogue. |\n\nUnknown record types encountered during adapter load must be\naccumulated into `Conversation.extensions.unknown_records[]` with\ntheir raw JSON — this is the resilience hook the locked plan calls\nfor. Don't silently ignore.\n\n## 4. Subagent decision\n\n**Two on-disk shapes observed for subagent sessions:**\n\n- **Old (pre-2.1.x?)**: `<project-dir>/agent-<hash>.jsonl` at the\n  project root. Example: the v2.0.76 sample #6. Records carry\n  `agentId` but no nested subdir.\n- **New (≥ 2.1.x)**: `<project-dir>/<parent-session-uuid>/subagents/agent-<name>-<hash>.jsonl`.\n  Example: the v2.1.51 sample #4.\n\nBoth carry the distinguishing field `agentId` on every record, and\nboth omit `version` information on some records (sample #6 did not\nemit `requestId` on user records, for instance — earlier Claude\nversions carried less metadata).\n\n**v0.1 decision: option (a) from the plan — ignore subagent JSONLs\nin `pconv list` and `pconv dump`.** Rationale:\n\n- Subagent sessions are transient reasoning loops, not user-facing\n  dialogues the user typically wants to paste-resume.\n- The parent session's `tool_use` / `tool_result` pair already\n  captures the subagent invocation and its consolidated output in\n  the main stream.\n- Surfacing subagents would require either a `subagent_of` field\n  (breaks the Conversation model shape) or a join (exposes\n  tool-call structure the schema is designed to hide behind\n  `ContentBlock::ToolUse`).\n\n**Detection rule** for the adapter's `list()`: skip any JSONL whose\npath contains `/subagents/` **or** whose filename matches\n`^agent-[a-z0-9_-]+\\.jsonl$` at the project root.\n\nRe-evaluate in v0.2+ — if users ask for \"show me what the subagent\nactually thought,\" option (b) (`subagent_of` in extensions) becomes\nthe natural add without reshaping the core model.\n\n## 5. Content-block variants\n\nObserved across the six samples:\n\n| Block `type` | Count across samples | v0.1 handling |\n|---|---:|---|\n| `text` | 120 | `ContentBlock::Text(String)` |\n| `tool_use` | 271 | `ContentBlock::ToolUse { id, name, input }` |\n| `tool_result` | 270 | `ContentBlock::ToolResult { tool_use_id, output, is_error }` |\n| `thinking` | 211 | `ContentBlock::Text` with a one-line prefix noting it was a thinking block. Rendering decision: paste output collapses thinking by default; `--include-thinking` opts in. |\n| `<string-content>` | 36 | When `message.content` is a bare JSON string instead of an array (older Claude versions do this on some user records), treat as a single `Text(String)` block. |\n| `<no-content>` | 13 | Observed on some `assistant` records with tool-only turns mid-stream. Normalize to an empty `Vec<ContentBlock>`; don't drop the message. |\n\n**Not observed in this sample but known to exist in Anthropic's API**:\n`image`, `document`, `redacted_thinking`. Adapter must accept them:\n\n- `image` → `ContentBlock::Text(\"<image omitted in v0.1>\")` with the\n  raw block stashed in the `Message.extensions.original_content[]`.\n- `document` → same passthrough.\n- `redacted_thinking` → dropped entirely, not even mentioned in\n  paste output (respects the redaction).\n\nAny other unknown block type goes to `Text(\"<unknown block: X>\")`\nwith the raw JSON in `message.extensions.original_content[]`.\n\n## 6. Path-content observations\n\nFeeds the later `--rewrite` transform design. Counts below are\nline-level presence (regex match anywhere in a record line), not\nstrict content-only substring counts; the real transform needs a\nstricter scope (prose text + tool-call args, not JSON field names or\n`cwd`). Noted as an open question in §7.\n\n| Sample | Lines with `/mnt/` | Lines with `X:\\\\` |\n|---|---:|---:|\n| #1 tiny | 0 | 0 |\n| #2 small WSL | 38 (90%) | 4 |\n| #3 medium Windows-encoded | 464 (95%) | 57 |\n| #4 subagent | 6 (100%) | 0 |\n| #5 large WSL | 800 (99%) | 158 |\n| #6 old-agent | 23 (100%) | 3 |\n\nKey observation: **the Windows-encoded bucket (#3) has 464 lines\nmentioning `/mnt/` paths but only 57 mentioning `C:\\\\`.** This is\nthe content-layer path-poisoning the research doc predicted —\nconfirmed at scale. A WSL-authored session lives in the\nWindows-encoded dir because it was launched from Windows once, but\nits content still carries WSL path references from the authoring\nside. Pure file-layer sync cannot fix this; `--rewrite wsl-to-win`\non this session's output is the right fix.\n\nSingle-session WSL-encoded files (#2, #5) also carry small numbers\nof `C:\\` references — 4 and 158. These are probably paste-ins from\nuser messages or web search results, not authored paths. The\nrewrite transform must not assume all encountered paths are\nrewritable.\n\n## 7. Open questions surfaced for Phase 2\n\nFlag these to the user before types are committed.\n\n1. **Multi-session JSONLs.** Sample #5 (20 MB) contained 2 distinct\n   `sessionId` values in one file. Spot-check suggests `/compact`\n   writes the continuation under a new session UUID but appends to\n   the same file. v0.1 adapter must decide:\n   - **(a)** `list()` surfaces every distinct `sessionId` seen,\n     `load(id)` filters to records matching that sessionId only; OR\n   - **(b)** `list()` surfaces only the file-level id (first\n     sessionId seen), `load()` returns the full file concatenated.\n   - Recommendation: **(a)**. Matches the Claude-side mental model\n     where `/resume` picks by sessionId, not by file.\n2. **Compact-summary record inclusion.** The `isCompactSummary: true`\n   user record carries the summarized prior session's text in\n   `message.content[0].text`. v0.1 treats this as a normal user\n   message. Confirm the user wants this (it can be 10+ KB of prose\n   that wasn't typed by the human). An `--exclude-compact-summaries`\n   flag may be worthwhile.\n3. **Path-rewrite scope.** §6 counted line-level hits as a proxy.\n   The real transform must target prose inside `text` blocks plus\n   tool-call `input` fields (e.g. `Read.file_path`) — **not** the\n   record's own `cwd` field, which is metadata describing where the\n   session ran. Spec this during Phase 2 before regex tuning.\n4. **Oldest Claude Code version supported.** Sample #6 (v2.0.76)\n   was missing `requestId` and `slug` fields on many records. v2.1.x\n   samples have them. The adapter must tolerate missing fields\n   gracefully. Worth picking an explicit floor (\"tested against\n   ≥ 2.0.x; earlier versions best-effort\").\n5. **`progress` record skip.** Confirm: does dropping all 204\n   `progress` records from sample #5 lose anything a paste-recovery\n   user would want? If the subagent ran a 5-step plan that only\n   showed up in progress streams (never in the final tool_result),\n   that context is gone. Spot-check one paste output to validate.\n\n## Appendix A — full top-level field set observed\n\nUnion across all six samples, for reference when building the\nserde structs:\n\n```\nagentId, compactMetadata, content, cwd, data, durationMs,\nerror, gitBranch, isApiErrorMessage, isCompactSummary, isMeta,\nisSidechain, isSnapshotUpdate, isVisibleInTranscriptOnly, level,\nlogicalParentUuid, message, messageId, operation, parentToolUseID,\nparentUuid, permissionMode, requestId, sessionId, slug, snapshot,\nsourceToolAssistantUUID, subtype, thinkingMetadata, timestamp,\ntodos, toolUseID, toolUseResult, type, userType, uuid, version\n```\n\nCore set the schema claims first-class: `uuid`, `parentUuid`,\n`sessionId`, `cwd`, `gitBranch`, `version`, `timestamp`, `type`,\n`message`. Everything else goes into extensions until a future\nadapter version promotes it.\n",

## Assistant

Phase 1 done. Both artifacts in place:

- **`docs/adapter-notes-claude-code.md`** — v0.1 adapter contract. 6 record types classified, subagent decision (option a, ignore both old + new shapes), content-block handling including unseen variants (`image`, `document`, `redacted_thinking`), path-poisoning confirmed at scale (Windows-encoded dir has 464/489 lines with `/mnt/` paths), 5 open questions for Phase 2.
- **`examples/scan-claude-jsonl.rs`** — throwaway parser, serde_json-only, streams via `BufRead::lines`. Ran all 6 samples (~22 MB) in 5.5s, zero parse errors.

Key surprises worth flagging before Phase 2:

1. **Single JSONL can hold multiple `sessionId`s** (sample #5 had 2) — `/compact` appears to write continuations under a new sessionId but appends to the same file. Adapter must filter by sessionId, not assume file=session.
2. **Two subagent on-disk shapes**, not one: old Claude (≤2.0.x) wrote `<proj>/agent-<hash>.jsonl` at root; new (≥2.1.x) writes `<proj>/<parent-uuid>/subagents/agent-<name>-<hash>.jsonl`. Both carry `agentId` — same concept, two locations. Detection rule in §4.
3. **`isCompactSummary` records** are regular `user` messages whose content is the compacted prior-session summary (sometimes 10+ KB of prose the human didn't type). Flagged as open question #2.

Also — noted the GitHub repo at https://github.com/cybersader/portaconv; Cargo.toml's `repository`/`homepage` already point there.

Ready for Phase 2 when you are. Want me to walk through the 5 open questions first, or just proceed with the schema/adapter skeleton and address them as they come up in code?

{
  "content": "---\ntitle: portaconv\ndescription: Terminal-native conversation extractor + MCP server for agent CLIs.\ntemplate: splash\nhero:\n  tagline: Extract any agent CLI's conversation history into paste-ready markdown. Normalize to OpenAI Chat Completions. Rewrite WSL ↔ Windows paths on the way out. Claude Code first; others follow.\n  actions:\n    - text: Get started\n      link: /portaconv/getting-started/installation/\n      icon: right-arrow\n    - text: View on GitHub\n      link: https://github.com/cybersader/portaconv\n      icon: external\n      variant: minimal\n---\n\nimport { Card, CardGrid, Aside } from \"@astrojs/starlight/components\";\n\n## Why\n\nAgent CLIs each keep conversation history in their own format, keyed\nto the absolute path of the directory the tool was launched from. Run\nClaude Code from WSL, then from Windows, and you get two\n`~/.claude/projects/` buckets for the same project — with **content**\nthat carries OS-specific absolute paths baked into `cwd`, `file_path`\ntool args, and prose. File-level sync can merge storage but cannot\nfix content-layer divergence.\n\n**portaconv** pivots away from sync and into **extract**. Pick a\nconversation, render it to paste-ready markdown, and drop it into\nany fresh agent session — Claude Code, opencode, claude.ai web, or\nthe API. Optionally rewrite paths on the way out.\n\n<Aside type=\"note\">\nNot a viewer. Not a daemon. Not a sync tool. A Unix-pipe-friendly\nextractor. If you want a GUI, [claude-code-history-viewer](https://github.com/jhlee0409/claude-code-history-viewer)\ncovers that niche well.\n</Aside>\n\n## Commands (v0.1)\n\n<CardGrid>\n  <Card title=\"pconv list\" icon=\"list-format\">\n    List conversations from any detected agent CLI. Filter by\n    workspace, time, or tool.\n  </Card>\n  <Card title=\"pconv dump\" icon=\"document\">\n    Dump one session to stdout as paste-ready markdown.\n    Opt-in `--rewrite wsl-to-win` / `win-to-wsl` / `strip` transforms.\n  </Card>\n  <Card title=\"pconv mcp serve\" icon=\"seti:config\">\n    Stdio MCP server. `list_conversations` + `get_conversation`\n    tools; each conversation exposed as `convos://conversation/&lt;id&gt;`.\n  </Card>\n</CardGrid>\n\n## How it composes\n\nportaconv is a sibling to [portagenty](https://github.com/cybersader/portagenty)\n(the terminal-native workspace launcher). Use them together or\nindependently:\n\n- **Standalone**: `cargo install portaconv`, run `pconv` from any\n  terminal. Reads `~/.claude/projects/` directly.\n- **With portagenty**: future `pa convos` shim passes workspace\n  context to `pconv` so list/dump automatically scope to the\n  current workspace's projects.\n\n## Status\n\n**v0.0.1 bootstrap.** Research spike complete — see the\n[Claude Code adapter notes](/portaconv/reference/adapter-claude-code/)\nfor the v0.1 contract.   "content": "---\ntitle: Concepts\ndescription: How portaconv thinks about conversation history.\nsidebar:\n  order: 1\n---\n\nportaconv sits between a handful of non-obvious ideas. Skim these\nbefore the reference.\n\n## Adapter\n\nA read-only normalizer for one agent CLI's on-disk conversation\nstorage. Each adapter implements a small trait: `detect()`, `list()`,\n`load(id)`. The adapter's job is to turn the tool's native format\ninto portaconv's shared `Conversation` model without losing anything\na renderer might care about later.\n\nThe v0.1 built-in is [Claude Code](/portaconv/reference/adapter-claude-code/).\nopencode, Cursor, Aider, and continue.dev are planned as separate PRs\nafter the trait survives contact with reality.\n\n## Shared conversation model\n\nOne `Conversation` type, tool-agnostic:\n\n- `messages: Vec<Message>` — ordered, with timestamps\n- Each message has a role (user / assistant / system / tool) and a\n  `Vec<ContentBlock>` (text / tool_use / tool_result / thinking)\n- A per-conversation `extensions: serde_json::Value` bag carries\n  tool-specific fields (Claude's `gitBranch`, `version`,\n  `permissionMode`, …) without polluting the core schema\n- Each message has its own `extensions` bag for the same reason\n\nShape is OpenAI Chat Completions on the outside, Anthropic\ncontent-blocks on the inside. That's the convergence point every\nserious tool already speaks.\n\n## Renderer\n\nTakes a `Conversation` and a format flag (`markdown` default, `json`,\n`plain`) and produces stdout. The default markdown shape is tuned\nfor pasting back into another agent — `## User` / `## Assistant`\nblocks, tool calls as fenced code, tool results truncated by default.\n\n## Path-rewrite transforms\n\nClaude Code JSONLs carry absolute filesystem paths from the authoring\nOS inside `cwd` fields, tool-call args, and prose. A session authored\nfrom WSL (`/mnt/c/Users/…`) pastes badly into a Windows-launched\nsession (`C:\\Users\\…`) and vice versa.\n\n`pconv dump --rewrite wsl-to-win` (or `win-to-wsl`, or `strip`) is\nthe opt-in transform that addresses this at the **content** layer —\nthe thing file-level sync approaches cannot fix.\n\n## MCP server\n\n`pconv mcp serve` exposes the same capabilities over stdio MCP:\n\n- Tools: `list_conversations`, `get_conversation(id)`\n- Resources: each conversation at `convos://conversation/<id>`\n\nA running agent can query portaconv to pull prior conversation\ncontext into its working memory. Minimal by design; the heavy\nlifting happens inside the CLI and the stored JSONLs.\n\n## Read-only, on-demand\n\nportaconv never writes to any tool's storage. There is no daemon,\nno file watcher, no auto-sync. Every `pconv` invocation reads the\ncurrent state of disk and emits output. Simpler to reason about,\neasier to reverse, composable with pipes.\n",
  "file_path": "/mnt/c/Users/Cybersader/Documents/1 Projects, Workspaces/portaconv/docs/src/content/docs/concepts/index.md"
}

Check the\n[repo](https://github.com/cybersader/portaconv) for progress.\n:::\n\n## `pconv list`\n\nList conversations discoverable on this machine.\n\n```sh\npconv list\npconv list --tool claude-code\npconv list --since 2d\npconv list --workspace <uuid>    # scope by portagenty workspace id (future)\n```\n\nIn v0.1 `--tool` always defaults to `claude-code`; other adapters\narrive in later releases.\n\n## `pconv dump <session-id>`\n\nRender one session to stdout.\n\n```sh\npconv dump 9decac91-1ead-4324-a777-6ff9a667faa3\npconv dump <id> --format json\npconv dump <id> --rewrite wsl-to-win     # /mnt/c/… → C:\\…\npconv dump <id> --rewrite win-to-wsl     # C:\\… → /mnt/c/…\npconv dump <id> --rewrite strip          # remove absolute paths\n```\n\nDefaults:\n\n- `--format markdown` — `## User` / `## Assistant` blocks, tool\n  calls as fenced code, tool results truncated.\n- No path rewriting. Opt in explicitly.\n- No trimming. `--tail <N>` and `--max-tokens <N>` planned.\n\n## `pconv mcp serve`\n\nStart a stdio MCP server exposing:\n\n- **Tool** `list_conversations(since?, workspace_id?, limit?)`\n- **Tool** `get_conversation(id, format=\"markdown\"|\"json\", rewrite?)`\n- **Resource** template `convos://conversation/<id>`\n\nAdd to your agent's `mcp.json`:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"mcpServers\": {\n    \"portaconv\": {\n      \"command\": \"pconv\",\n      \"args\": [\"mcp\", \"serve\"]\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Non-goals for v0.1\n\n- No `pconv copy` (clipboard integration — v0.2).\n- No `pconv export --to <file>` (committable handoff docs — v0.2).\n- No search / FTS / embeddings — get-by-id only.\n- No writes back to any tool's storage. Ever. Read-only by design.\n",

```json
{
  "content": "---\ntitle: Claude Code adapter notes\ndescription: The v0.1 contract for how portaconv reads ~/.claude/projects/ JSONLs.\nsidebar:\n  order: 2\n---\n\nEmpirical freeze of what the Claude Code adapter handles in portaconv\nv0.1, based on a spike against six real JSONLs pulled from\n`~/.claude/projects/` on 2026-04-20 (host: Linux/WSL, Claude Code\nversions 2.0.76 → 2.1.51 observed).\n\nThe adapter trait and schema types get committed in Phase 2 against\nthis contract.\n\n## 1. Scope\n\n- Normative: any record type listed in §3 is handled as specified.\n- Any record type not listed is **unknown** — the adapter must not\n  silently drop it; it must either land in a per-record\n  `extensions: serde_json::Value` bag or flip a one-line warning.\n- The schema contract itself (`Conversation` / `Message` /\n  `ContentBlock`) is locked in the project's\n  [design decisions](https://github.com/cybersader/portaconv/blob/main/knowledgebase/03-design-decisions.md);\n  this doc does not reopen it. It only defines the adapter's mapping\n  onto it.\n\n## 2. Sample inventory\n\nSix JSONLs, spread across size, OS encoding, and on-disk shape.\nParser: `examples/scan-claude-jsonl.rs` (throwaway, deleted before\nPhase 2 lands).\n\n| # | Slot | Size | Lines | Encoded dir (prefix) | Filename shape | Claude ver(s) |\n|---|------|-----:|------:|---------------------|----------------|---------------|\n| 1 | Tiny | 708 B | 3 | `-mnt-c-…-<proj-f>` | `<uuid>.jsonl` | (no version field in records) |\n| 2 | Small WSL | 100 KB | 42 | `-mnt-c-…-<proj-b>` | `<uuid>.jsonl` | 2.1.39, 2.1.42 |\n| 3 | Medium Win | 995 KB | 489 | `C--…-<proj-d>` | `<uuid>.jsonl` | 2.1.20 |\n| 4 | Subagent (new) | 11 KB | 6 | `-mnt-c-…-<proj-e>/<parent-uuid>/subagents/` | `agent-acompact-<hash>.jsonl` | 2.1.51 |\n| 5 | Large | 19.8 MB | 805 | `-mnt-c-…-<proj-c>` | `<uuid>.jsonl` | 2.1.2, 2.1.9 |\n| 6 | Agent (old) | 80 KB | 23 | `-mnt-c-…-<client-a-project>` | `agent-<hash>.jsonl` | 2.0.76 |\n\nStreaming line-parse completed all six (≈22 MB combined) in **5.5 s\nwall-time** — well under the \"seconds not minutes\" bar the plan set.\nZero parse errors across 1368 records.\n\n## 3. Record type table\n\nThe top-level `type` discriminator has six values in this sample.\n\n| `type` | Description | Bucket | v0.1 handling | Notes |\n|---|---|---|---|---|\n| `user` | Conversational message, user role. `message.{role, content[]}` is the event-stream shape. | **Schema** | Map to `Message { role: User, content: Vec<ContentBlock>, timestamp, extensions }`. Copy top-level `uuid`, `parentUuid`, `requestId`, `isSidechain`, `slug`, `userType` into `message.extensions`. | Includes compact-summary records (`isCompactSummary: true`) — those are regular `user` records whose content is the summary text. Keep them. |\n| `assistant` | Conversational message, assistant role. Same event-stream shape. | **Schema** | Same as `user`. Content includes `tool_use` and `thinking` blocks alongside `text`. | `thinkingMetadata` on the record goes into `message.extensions`. |\n| `system` | Metadata event (e.g. `subtype: \"turn_duration\"` with `durationMs`). No `message.content`. | **Extensions** (conv-level) | Append as-is to `Conversation.extensions.system_events[]` (append-only array). Do not render to paste output in v0.1. | Only 6–9 per long session. Small. |\n| `file-history-snapshot` | Claude Code's file-tracking metadata: `{messageId, snapshot: {trackedFileBackups, timestamp}, isSnapshotUpdate}`. | **Skip** | Drop. Not surfaced in `Conversation.extensions`. | These files are tracked elsewhere in Claude's workspace; portaconv is not a file-state tool. |\n| `progress` | Live streaming events for subagent runs. Carries `data.{message, type: \"agent_progress\", prompt, agentId}` + `toolUseID` + `parentToolUseID`. | **Skip** | Drop. | The final assistant message already carries the consolidated `tool_use`; the stream is transient. Re-evaluate if v0.1 paste output looks lossy on subagent-heavy sessions. |\n| `queue-operation` | Claude Code's prompt-queue bookkeeping (`operation: \"enqueue\"`, raw user-typed `content`). | **Skip** | Drop. | Internal scheduling state; not part of the rendered dialogue. |\n\nUnknown record types encountered during adapter load must be\naccumulated into `Conversation.extensions.unknown_records[]` with\ntheir raw JSON — this is the resilience hook the locked plan calls\nfor. Don't silently ignore.\n\n## 4. Subagent decision\n\n**Two on-disk shapes observed for subagent sessions:**\n\n- **Old (pre-2.1.x?)**: `<project-dir>/agent-<hash>.jsonl` at the\n  project root. Example: the v2.0.76 sample #6. Records carry\n  `agentId` but no nested subdir.\n- **New (≥ 2.1.x)**: `<project-dir>/<parent-session-uuid>/subagents/agent-<name>-<hash>.jsonl`.\n  Example: the v2.1.51 sample #4.\n\nBoth carry the distinguishing field `agentId` on every record, and\nboth omit `version` information on some records (sample #6 did not\nemit `requestId` on user records, for instance — earlier Claude\nversions carried less metadata).\n\n**v0.1 decision: option (a) from the plan — ignore subagent JSONLs\nin `pconv list` and `pconv dump`.** Rationale:\n\n- Subagent sessions are transient reasoning loops, not user-facing\n  dialogues the user typically wants to paste-resume.\n- The parent session's `tool_use` / `tool_result` pair already\n  captures the subagent invocation and its consolidated output in\n  the main stream.\n- Surfacing subagents would require either a `subagent_of` field\n  (breaks the Conversation model shape) or a join (exposes\n  tool-call structure the schema is designed to hide behind\n  `ContentBlock::ToolUse`).\n\n**Detection rule** for the adapter's `list()`: skip any JSONL whose\npath contains `/subagents/` **or** whose filename matches\n`^agent-[a-z0-9_-]+\\.jsonl$` at the project root.\n\nRe-evaluate in v0.2+ — if users ask for \"show me what the subagent\nactually thought,\" option (b) (`subagent_of` in extensions) becomes\nthe natural add without reshaping the core model.\n\n## 5. Content-block variants\n\nObserved across the six samples:\n\n| Block `type` | Count across samples | v0.1 handling |\n|---|---:|---|\n| `text` | 120 | `ContentBlock::Text(String)` |\n| `tool_use` | 271 | `ContentBlock::ToolUse { id, name, input }` |\n| `tool_result` | 270 | `ContentBlock::ToolResult { tool_use_id, output, is_error }` |\n| `thinking` | 211 | `ContentBlock::Text` with a one-line prefix noting it was a thinking block. Rendering decision: paste output collapses thinking by default; `--include-thinking` opts in. |\n| `<string-content>` | 36 | When `message.content` is a bare JSON string instead of an array (older Claude versions do this on some user records), treat as a single `Text(String)` block. |\n| `<no-content>` | 13 | Observed on some `assistant` records with tool-only turns mid-stream. Normalize to an empty `Vec<ContentBlock>`; don't drop the message. |\n\n**Not observed in this sample but known to exist in Anthropic's API**:\n`image`, `document`, `redacted_thinking`. Adapter must accept them:\n\n- `image` → `ContentBlock::Text(\"<image omitted in v0.1>\")` with the\n  raw block stashed in the `Message.extensions.original_content[]`.\n- `document` → same passthrough.\n- `redacted_thinking` → dropped entirely, not even mentioned in\n  paste output (respects the redaction).\n\nAny other unknown block type goes to `Text(\"<unknown block: X>\")`\nwith the raw JSON in `message.extensions.original_content[]`.\n\n## 6. Path-content observations\n\nFeeds the later `--rewrite` transform design. Counts below are\nline-level presence (regex match anywhere in a record line), not\nstrict content-only substring counts; the real transform needs a\nstricter scope (prose text + tool-call args, not JSON field names or\n`cwd`). Noted as an open question in §7.\n\n| Sample | Lines with `/mnt/` | Lines with `X:\\\\` |\n|---|---:|---:|\n| #1 tiny | 0 | 0 |\n| #2 small WSL | 38 (90%) | 4 |\n| #3 medium Windows-encoded | 464 (95%) | 57 |\n| #4 subagent | 6 (100%) | 0 |\n| #5 large WSL | 800 (99%) | 158 |\n| #6 old-agent | 23 (100%) | 3 |\n\nKey observation: **the Windows-encoded bucket (#3) has 464 lines\nmentioning `/mnt/` paths but only 57 mentioning `C:\\\\`.** This is\nthe content-layer path-poisoning the research doc predicted —\nconfirmed at scale. A WSL-authored session lives in the\nWindows-encoded dir because it was launched from Windows once, but\nits content still carries WSL path references from the authoring\nside. Pure file-layer sync cannot fix this; `--rewrite wsl-to-win`\non this session's output is the right fix.\n\nSingle-session WSL-encoded files (#2, #5) also carry small numbers\nof `C:\\` references — 4 and 158. These are probably paste-ins from\nuser messages or web search results, not authored paths. The\nrewrite transform must not assume all encountered paths are\nrewritable.\n\n## 7. Open questions surfaced for Phase 2\n\nFlag these to the user before types are committed.\n\n1. **Multi-session JSONLs.** Sample #5 (20 MB) contained 2 distinct\n   `sessionId` values in one file. Spot-check suggests `/compact`\n   writes the continuation under a new session UUID but appends to\n   the same file. v0.1 adapter must decide:\n   - **(a)** `list()` surfaces every distinct `sessionId` seen,\n     `load(id)` filters to records matching that sessionId only; OR\n   - **(b)** `list()` surfaces only the file-level id (first\n     sessionId seen), `load()` returns the full file concatenated.\n   - Recommendation: **(a)**. Matches the Claude-side mental model\n     where `/resume` picks by sessionId, not by file.\n2. **Compact-summary record inclusion.** The `isCompactSummary: true`\n   user record carries the summarized prior session's text in\n   `message.content[0].text`. v0.1 treats this as a normal user\n   message. Confirm the user wants this (it can be 10+ KB of prose\n   that wasn't typed by the human). An `--exclude-compact-summaries`\n   flag may be worthwhile.\n3. **Path-rewrite scope.** §6 counted line-level hits as a proxy.\n   The real transform must target prose inside `text` blocks plus\n   tool-call `input` fields (e.g. `Read.file_path`) — **not** the\n   record's own `cwd` field, which is metadata describing where the\n   session ran. Spec this during Phase 2 before regex tuning.\n4. **Oldest Claude Code version supported.** Sample #6 (v2.0.76)\n   was missing `requestId` and `slug` fields on many records. v2.1.x\n   samples have them. The adapter must tolerate missing fields\n   gracefully. Worth picking an explicit floor (\"tested against\n   ≥ 2.0.x; earlier versions best-effort\").\n5. **`progress` record skip.** Confirm: does dropping all 204\n   `progress` records from sample #5 lose anything a paste-recovery\n   user would want? If the subagent ran a 5-step plan that only\n   showed up in progress streams (never in the final tool_result),\n   that context is gone. Spot-check one paste output to validate.\n\n## Appendix A — full top-level field set observed\n\nUnion across all six samples, for reference when building the\nserde structs:\n\n```\nagentId, compactMetadata, content, cwd, data, durationMs,\nerror, gitBranch, isApiErrorMessage, isCompactSummary, isMeta,\nisSidechain, isSnapshotUpdate, isVisibleInTranscriptOnly, level,\nlogicalParentUuid, message, messageId, operation, parentToolUseID,\nparentUuid, permissionMode, requestId, sessionId, slug, snapshot,\nsourceToolAssistantUUID, subtype, thinkingMetadata, timestamp,\ntodos, toolUseID, toolUseResult, type, userType, uuid, version\n```\n\nCore set the schema claims first-class: `uuid`, `parentUuid`,\n`sessionId`, `cwd`, `gitBranch`, `version`, `timestamp`, `type`,\n`message`. Everything else goes into extensions until a future\nadapter version promotes it.\n",
  "file_path": "/mnt/c/Users/Cybersader/Documents/1 Projects, Workspaces/portaconv/docs/src/content/docs/reference/adapter-claude-code.md"
}

```json
{
  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env node\n/**\n * portaconv docs serve — interactive menu for local docs preview + sharing.\n *\n *   bun run serve              — interactive menu\n *   bun run serve dev          — Astro dev server with HMR (LAN-bindable)\n *   bun run serve preview      — build docs + serve dist (production preview)\n *   bun run serve build        — docs build only → docs/dist\n *   bun run serve tailscale    — Astro dev shared via Tailscale (tailnet only)\n *   bun run serve cloudflare   — Astro dev shared via Cloudflare Tunnel (public)\n *\n * Pattern ported from sibling repo portagenty/docs/scripts/serve.mjs.\n * Covers the cross-OS rollup-binary contamination problem (WSL ↔ Windows)\n * and the local Tailscale share workflow.\n */\n\nimport { spawn, execSync } from \"node:child_process\";\nimport { existsSync, rmSync, statSync } from \"node:fs\";\nimport { resolve, dirname, join } from \"node:path\";\nimport { fileURLToPath } from \"node:url\";\nimport { createInterface } from \"node:readline\";\n\nconst __dirname = dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));\nconst docsDir = resolve(__dirname, \"..\");\nconst distDir = resolve(docsDir, \"dist\");\n\nconst DOCS_PORT = 4321;\nconst PREFIX = \"/portaconv\";\nconst isWindows = process.platform === \"win32\";\n\nlet staticServer = null;\n\nconst mode = process.argv[2] || \"interactive\";\nconst children = [];\n\nfunction log(msg) {\n  console.log(`  ${msg}`);\n}\nfunction sleep(ms) {\n  return new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, ms));\n}\n\nfunction run(cmd) {\n  try {\n    return execSync(cmd, { stdio: \"pipe\", timeout: 30000, shell: true })\n      .toString()\n      .trim();\n  } catch {\n    return \"\";\n  }\n}\n\nfunction hasCmd(name) {\n  return isWindows\n    ? !!run(`where ${name} 2>nul`)\n    : !!run(`which ${name} 2>/dev/null`);\n}\n\n// Rollup ships its native binary as a per-platform optional dep. If\n// docs/node_modules was installed on a different OS (e.g. WSL → Windows), the\n// wrong binary is present and astro dev crashes with\n// \"Cannot find module @rollup/rollup-<platform>\". Detect and force a clean\n// reinstall when that happens.\nfunction rollupNativePkg() {\n  const { platform, arch } = process;\n  if (platform === \"win32\" && arch === \"x64\")\n    return \"@rollup/rollup-win32-x64-msvc\";\n  if (platform === \"win32\" && arch === \"arm64\")\n    return \"@rollup/rollup-win32-arm64-msvc\";\n  if (platform === \"linux\" && arch === \"x64\")\n    return \"@rollup/rollup-linux-x64-gnu\";\n  if (platform === \"linux\" && arch === \"arm64\")\n    return \"@rollup/rollup-linux-arm64-gnu\";\n  if (platform === \"darwin\" && arch === \"x64\") return \"@rollup/rollup-darwin-x64\";\n  if (platform === \"darwin\" && arch === \"arm64\")\n    return \"@rollup/rollup-darwin-arm64\";\n  return null;\n}\n\nfunction ensureDocsDeps() {\n  const nodeModules = resolve(docsDir, \"node_modules\");\n  let needsInstall = false;\n  let needsNuke = false;\n\n  if (!existsSync(nodeModules)) {\n    needsInstall = true;\n  } else {\n    const expectedRollup = rollupNativePkg();\n    if (expectedRollup && !existsSync(resolve(nodeModules, expectedRollup))) {\n      log(\n        `docs/node_modules is missing ${expectedRollup} — likely installed on a different OS.`,\n      );\n      needsNuke = true;\n      needsInstall = true;\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (needsNuke) {\n    log(\"Removing stale docs/node_modules...\");\n    rmSync(nodeModules, { recursive: true, force: true });\n    const lock = resolve(docsDir, \"bun.lock\");\n    if (existsSync(lock)) {\n      log(\"Removing docs/bun.lock...\");\n      rmSync(lock, { force: true });\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (needsInstall) {\n    log(\"Installing docs/ dependencies (bun install)...\");\n    execSync(\"bun install\", { cwd: docsDir, stdio: \"inherit\", shell: true });\n    log(\"docs dependencies installed.\");\n  }\n}\n\nfunction getTailscale() {\n  if (hasCmd(\"tailscale\")) return \"tailscale\";\n  if (hasCmd(\"tailscale.exe\")) return \"tailscale.exe\";\n  return null;\n}\n\nfunction hasCloudflared() {\n  return hasCmd(\"cloudflared\") || !!run(\"bun x cloudflared --version 2>/dev/null\");\n}\n\nfunction track(child) {\n  children.push(child);\n  return child;\n}\n\nfunction cleanup() {\n  for (const c of children) {\n    try {\n      c.kill();\n    } catch {}\n  }\n  if (staticServer) {\n    try {\n      staticServer.stop(true);\n    } catch {}\n    staticServer = null;\n  }\n  const ts = getTailscale();\n  // `reset` is the modern (1.50+) verb to tear down all serves; the older\n  // `serve off` was deprecated and errors with \"handler does not exist\"\n  // when nothing is currently being served.\n  if (ts) run(`${ts} serve reset 2>/dev/null`);\n}\n\n// MIME / static-server pair shared by tailscale + cloudflare share modes.\nconst MIME = \".svg\": \"image/svg+xml\",\n  \".png\": \"image/png\",\n  \".jpg\": \"image/jpeg\",\n  \".jpeg\": \"image/jpeg\",\n  \".gif\": \"image/gif\",\n  \".webp\": \"image/webp\",\n  \".ico\": \"image/x-icon\",\n  \".xml\": \"application/xml\",\n  \".txt\": \"text/plain; charset=utf-8\",\n  \".woff\": \"font/woff\",\n  \".woff2\": \"font/woff2\",\n};\nfunction contentType(p) {\n  return MIME[p.slice(p.lastIndexOf(\".\"))] || \"application/octet-stream\";\n}\n\nfunction startStaticServer(port) {\n  log(`Starting static server (Bun.serve) on http://127.0.0.1:${port}...`);\n  staticServer = Bun.serve({\n    hostname: \"127.0.0.1\",\n    port,\n    fetch(req) {\n      const url = new URL(req.url);\n      let pathname = decodeURIComponent(url.pathname);\n      // Strip the configured Astro base so local paths mirror what GitHub\n      // Pages does in production (Astro emits absolute URLs with the base\n      // prefix, but writes files to dist/ without it).\n      if (pathname === PREFIX || pathname.startsWith(`${PREFIX}/`)) {\n        pathname = pathname.slice(PREFIX.length) || \"/\";\n      }\n      let filePath = join(distDir, pathname);\n      try {\n        if (existsSync(filePath) && statSync(filePath).isDirectory()) {\n          filePath = join(filePath, \"index.html\");\n        }\n        if (!existsSync(filePath)) {\n          if (existsSync(`${filePath}.html`)) {\n            filePath = `${filePath}.html`;\n          } else {\n            return new Response(\"Not found\", { status: 404 });\n          }\n        }\n        return new Response(Bun.file(filePath), {\n          headers: { \"Content-Type\": contentType(filePath) },\n        });\n      } catch (err) {\n        return new Response(`Error: ${err.message}`, { status: 500 });\n      }\n    },\n  });\n  log(`Static server ready.`);\n}\n\nprocess.on(\"SIGINT\", () => {\n  cleanup();\n  process.exit(0);\n});\nprocess.on(\"SIGTERM\", () => {\n  cleanup();\n  process.exit(0);\n});\n\nasync function prompt() {\n  const rl = createInterface({ input: process.stdin, output: process.stdout });\n  const ts = getTailscale();\n  const cf = hasCloudflared();\n\n  console.log(\"\\n  ━━━ portaconv docs serve ━━━\\n\");\n  console.log(`  1) Dev server (HMR)         http://localhost:${DOCS_PORT}`);\n  console.log(`  2) Preview built site       http://localhost:${DOCS_PORT}`);\n  console.log(`  3) Build only               → docs/dist`);\n  console.log(\n    `  4) Share via Tailscale      ${ts ? \"tailnet only\" : \"(not installed)\"}`,\n  );\n  console.log(\n    `  5) Share via Cloudflare     ${cf ? \"public URL\" : \"(cloudflared not found)\"}\\n`,\n  );\n\n  return new Promise((res) => {\n    rl.question(\"  Choose [1-5]: \", (a) => [\n        \"x\",\n        \"astro\",\n        \"dev\",\n        \"--host\",\n        \"0.0.0.0\",\n        \"--port\",\n        String(DOCS_PORT),\n      ],\n      { cwd: docsDir, stdio: \"inherit\", shell: isWindows },\n    ),\n  );\n  child.on(\"exit\", (code) => {\n    if (code !== 0 && code !== null) {\n      console.error(`\\n  Dev server exited with code ${code}`);\n      cleanup();\n      process.exit(code);\n    }\n  });\n  return child;\n}\n\nfunction startPreview() {\n  ensureDocsDeps();\n  log(\"Building docs site...\");\n  const build = spawn(\"bun\", [\"x\", \"astro\", \"build\"], {\n    cwd: docsDir,\n    stdio: \"inherit\",\n    shell: isWindows,\n  });\n  return new Promise((res, rej) => {\n    build.on(\"exit\", (code) => {\n      if (code !== 0) return rej(new \"inherit\", shell: isWindows },\n        ),\n      );\n      res();\n    });\n  });\n}\n\nfunction runBuild() {\n  ensureDocsDeps();\n  log(\"Building docs site → docs/dist...\");\n  return new Promise((res, rej) => {\n    const p = spawn(\"bun\", [\"x\", \"astro\", \"build\"], {\n      cwd: docsDir,\n      stdio: \"inherit\",\n      shell: isWindows,\n    });\n    p.on(\"exit\", (code) => {\n      if (code !== 0) return rej(new Error(`build failed (exit ${code})`));\n      log(\"Build complete.\");\n      res();\n    });\n  });\n}\n\nasync function waitForLocalReady(port, timeoutMs) {\n  const url = `http://127.0.0.1:${port}${PREFIX}/`;\n  const deadline = Date.now() + timeoutMs;\n  log(`Waiting for dev server at ${url}...`);\n  while (Date.now() < deadline) {\n    try {\n tailscaleServe(port) {\n  const ts = getTailscale();\n  if (!ts) {\n    log(\"Tailscale not found. Install it from https://tailscale.com.\");\n    return;\n  }\n  run(`${ts} serve reset 2>/dev/null`);\n  run(`${ts} serve --bg ${port}`);\n  await sleep(1500);\n  const status = run(`${ts} serve status 2>/dev/null`);\n  const url = status.match(/(https:\\/\\/[^\\s]+\\.ts\\.net)/)?.[1];\n  const ip = run(`${ts} ip -4 2>/dev/null`);\n  console.log(\"\");\n  if (url) log(`Public-on-tailnet: ${url}${PREFIX}/`);\n  if (ip) log(`Direct: http://${ip}:${port}${PREFIX}/ (tailnet only)`);\n  if (!url && !ip) log(`http://localhost:${port}${PREFIX}/`);\n  log(`Stop sharing: tailscale serve reset`);\n}\n\nfunction startCloudflareTunnel(port) {\n  log(\"Starting Cloudflare Tunnel...\");\n  return track(\n    spawn(\n      \"bun\",\n      [\"x\", \"cloudflared\", \"tunnel\", \"--url\", `http://localhost:${port}`],\n      { stdio: \"inherit\", shell: isWindows },\n    ),\n  );\n}\n\nasync function main() {\n  const chosen = mode === \"interactive\" ? await prompt() : mode;\n\n  switch (chosen) {\n    case \"dev\":\n      startDev();\n      break;\n    case \"preview\":\n      await startPreview();\n      break;\n    case \"build\":\n      await runBuild();\n      process.exit(0);\n    case \"tailscale\":\n      await runBuild();\n      startStaticServer(DOCS_PORT);\n      await waitForLocalReady(DOCS_PORT, 10_000);\n      await tailscaleServe(DOCS_PORT);\n      log(\"Press Ctrl+C to stop sharing.\");\n      await new Promise(() => {});\n      break;\n    case \"cloudflare\":\n      await runBuild();\n      startStaticServer(DOCS_PORT);\n      await waitForLocalReady(DOCS_PORT, 10_000);\n      startCloudflareTunnel(DOCS_PORT);\n      log(\"Press Ctrl+C to stop sharing.\");\n      await new Promise(() => {});\n      break;\n    default:\n      console.error(`Unknown mode: ${chosen}`);\n      console.error(\n        \"Use one of: dev, preview, build, tailscale, cloudflare (or no arg for menu)\",\n      );\n      process.exit(1);\n  }\n}\n\nmain().catch((err) => {\n  console.error(err);\n  cleanup();\n  process.exit(1);\n});\n",

  failures++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    if (status !== 200) {\n      console.error(`  FAIL  ${path} — expected 200, got ${status}`);\n      failures++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    if ```
Rule of thumb: **sync script only when content legitimately belongs in another location and shouldn't be duplicated**. Don't add one for convenience.

## Deploy

GitHub Pages via Actions. Boilerplate workflow:

- Build on push to `main` affecting `docs/**` (or site equivalent)
- Setup bun + node 22
- `bun install && bun run build`
- Upload `dist/` as artifact
- Deploy via `actions/deploy-pages@v4`

For repo + site naming:

- If site is at repo root: deploy to `cybersader.github.io/<repo>/`
- Config the `base` path in `astro.config.mjs` to match

**tool call:** `Write`

```json
{
  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env bun\n/**\n * Visual iteration harness — serves dist/ statically, launches chromium,\n * navigates to a Starlight page, inspects the page structure, and\n * screenshots the full page.\n *\n * Pattern ported from mcp-workflow-and-tech-stack/site/scripts/visual.mjs\n * (which inspects a graph component); here simplified for plain Starlight\n * pages — no graph/canvas, just navigation, error-capture, screenshots.\n *\n * Usage:\n *   bun scripts/visual.mjs                                  # default: / on mobile viewport\n *   bun scripts/visual.mjs /reference/adapter-claude-code/  # specific page\n *   bun scripts/visual.mjs / desktop                        # desktop viewport\n *   bun scripts/visual.mjs / mobile keep                    # keep open after screenshot\n *\n * Outputs to /tmp/pconv-visual-<timestamp>/:\n *   - full.png    Full-page screenshot\n *   - report.md   DOM inspection, console logs, page errors\n *\n * Requires `dist/` to exist — run `bun run build` (or `bun run serve build`)\n * first. Visual is for inspection, not for CI; use smoke.mjs for CI.\n */\n\nimport { existsSync, statSync, mkdirSync } from \"node:fs\";\nimport { writeFile } from \"node:fs/promises\";\nimport { resolve, dirname, join } from \"node:path\";\nimport { fileURLToPath } from \"node:url\";\nimport { chromium } from \"playwright\";\n\nconst __dirname = dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));\nconst docsDir = resolve(__dirname, \"..\");\nconst distDir = resolve(docsDir, \"dist\");\n\nconst PATH = process.argv[2] || \"/\";\nconst VIEWPORT_MODE = process.argv[3] || \"mobile\";\nconst KEEP = process.argv.includes(\"keep\");\n\nconst PORT = 4323;\nconst PREFIX = \"/portaconv\";\n\nconst VIEWPORTS = {\n  mobile: { width: 390, height: 844 },\n  tablet: { width: 768, height: 1024 },\n  narrow: { width: 1024, height: 768 },\n  desktop: { width: 1440, height: 900 },\n};\nconst viewport = VIEWPORTS[VIEWPORT_MODE] || VIEWPORTS.mobile;\n\nif (!existsSync(distDir)) {\n  console.error(`  ERROR: ${distDir} does not exist — run \\`bun run build\\` first.`);\n  process.exit(1);\n}\n\nconst MIME = {\n  \".html\": \"text/html; charset=utf-8\",\n  \".js\": \"application/javascript\",\n  \".mjs\": \"application/javascript\",\n  \".css\": \"text/css\",\n  \".json\": \"application/json\",\n  \".svg\": \"image/svg+xml\",\n  \".png\": \"image/png\",\n  \".jpg\": \"image/jpeg\",\n  \".jpeg\": \"image/jpeg\",\n  \".gif\": \"image/gif\",\n  \".webp\": \"image/webp\",\n  \".ico\": \"image/x-icon\",\n  \".xml\": \"application/xml\",\n  \".txt\": \"text/plain; charset=utf-8\",\n  \".woff\": \"font/woff\",\n  \".woff2\": \"font/woff2\",\n};\nconst contentType = (p) =>\n  MIME[p.slice(p.lastIndexOf(\".\"))] || \"application/octet-stream\";\n\n// ── Static server ────────────────────────────────────────────────────\nconst server = Bun.serve({\n  hostname: \"127.0.0.1\",\n  port: PORT,\n  fetch(req) {\n    const url = new URL(req.url);\n    let pathname = decodeURIComponent(url.pathname);\n    if (pathname === PREFIX || pathname.startsWith(`${PREFIX}/`)) {\n      pathname = pathname.slice(PREFIX.length) || \"/\";\n    }\n    let filePath = join(distDir, pathname);\n    try {\n      if (existsSync(filePath) && statSync(filePath).isDirectory()) {\n        filePath = join(filePath, \"index.html\");\n      }\n      if (!existsSync(filePath)) {\n        if (existsSync(`${filePath}.html`)) filePath = `${filePath}.html`;\n        else return new Response(\"Not found\", { status: 404 });\n      }\n      return new Response(Bun.file(filePath), {\n        headers: { \"Content-Type\": contentType(filePath) },\n      });\n    } catch (err) {\n      return new Response(`Error: ${err.message}`, { status: 500 });\n    }\n  },\n});\n\nconsole.log(`  Static server on http://127.0.0.1:${PORT}`);\nconsole.log(\n  `  Target: ${PATH} @ ${VIEWPORT_MODE} (${viewport.width}x${viewport.height})`,\n);\n\nconst outDir = `/tmp/pconv-visual-${Date.now()}`;\nmkdirSync(outDir, { recursive: true });\nconsole.log(`  Output: ${outDir}`);\n\n// ── Browser + inspect ────────────────────────────────────────────────\nconst browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });\nconst context = await browser.newContext({ viewport });\nconst page = await context.newPage();\n\nconst consoleLogs = [];\nconst pageErrors = [];\npage.on(\"console\", (msg) => {\n  consoleLogs.push({ type: msg.type(), text: msg.text() });\n});\npage.on(\"pageerror\", (err) => pageErrors.push(err.message));\n\nconst url = `http://127.0.0.1:${PORT}${PREFIX}${PATH}`;\nconsole.log(`  Navigating to ${url}`);\nconst response = await page.goto(url, {\n  waitUntil: \"networkidle\",\n  timeout: 30_000,\n});\nconst httpStatus = response ? response.status() : 0;\nconsole.log(`  HTTP ${httpStatus}`);\n\n// ── Starlight page inspection ────────────────────────────────────────\nconst inspection = await page.evaluate(() => {\n  const result = {};\n\n  result.title = document.title;\n  result.metaDescription =\n    document.querySelector('meta[name=\"description\"]')?.getAttribute(\"content\") ||\n    null;\n\n  const header = document.querySelector(\"header.header\");\n  result.header = {\n    found: !!header,\n    siteTitle:\n      document.querySelector('a[href][rel=\"home\"]')?.textContent?.trim() ||\n      document.querySelector(\".site-title\")?.textContent?.trim() ||\n      null,\n  };\n\n  const sidebar = document.querySelector(\"nav.sidebar, .sidebar-content\");\n  result.sidebar = {\n    found: !!sidebar,\n    groupCount: document.querySelectorAll(\".sidebar nav ul > li, .large\").length,\n    linkCount: document.querySelectorAll(\".sidebar a[href]\").length,\n  };\n\n  const main = document.querySelector(\"main\");\n  result.main = {\n    found: !!main,\n    h1: main?.querySelector(\"h1\")?.textContent?.trim() || null,\n    h2Count: main?.querySelectorAll(\"h2\").length || 0,\n    h3Count: main?.querySelectorAll(\"h3\").length || 0,\n    tableCount: main?.querySelectorAll(\"table\").length || 0,\n    codeBlockCount: main?.querySelectorAll(\"pre > code\").length || 0,\n    textLength: main?.textContent?.trim().length || 0,\n  };\n\n  // Flexoki theme loaded = CSS var --sl-color-accent is present.\n  const root = getComputedStyle(document.documentElement);\n  result.theme = {\n    slColorAccent: root.getPropertyValue(\"--sl-color-accent\").trim(),\n    slColorBg: root.getPropertyValue(\"--sl-color-bg\").trim(),\n  };\n\n  // Pagefind search wiring.\n  result.pagefind = {\n    searchEl: !!document.querySelector(\n      '[data-pagefind-search], #starlight__search, [data-pagefind-ui]',\n    ),\n  };\n\n  // Broken-image detection — any <img> that failed to load.\n  const broken = Array.from(document.images)\n    .filter((img) => img.complete && img.naturalWidth === 0)\n    .map((img) => img.src);\n  result.brokenImages = broken;\n\n  return result;\n});\n\nconsole.log(`\\n  === Inspection ===`);\nconsole.log(JSON.stringify(inspection, null, 2));\n\n// ── Screenshots ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────\nawait page.screenshot({ path: join(outDir, \"full.png\"), fullPage: true });\nconsole.log(`  Saved: ${outDir}/full.png`);\n\n// ── Report ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\nconst errorBlock = [\n  `## Page errors`,\n  ...(pageErrors.length ? pageErrors.map((e) => `- ${e}`) : [\"(none)\"]),\n  ``,\n  `## Console logs`,\n  `Total: ${consoleLogs.length}`,\n  ...consoleLogs.slice(0, 30).map((l) => `- [${l.type}] ${l.text}`),\n];\n\nconst report = [\n  `# pconv visual report`,\n  ``,\n  `- URL: ${url}`,\n  `- HTTP status: ${httpStatus}`,\n  `- Viewport: ${VIEWPORT_MODE} (${viewport.width}x${viewport.height})`,\n  `- Timestamp: ${new Date().toISOString()}`,\n  ``,\n  `## Page metadata`,\n  `- title: ${inspection.title}`,\n  `- description: ${inspection.metaDescription}`,\n  ``,\n  `## Starlight structure`,\n  `\\`\\`\\`json`,\n  JSON.stringify(\n    { header: inspection.header, sidebar: inspection.sidebar, main: inspection.main },\n    null,\n    2,\n  ),\n  `\\`\\`\\``,\n  ``,\n  `## Theme tokens`,\n  `\\`\\`\\`json`,\n  JSON.stringify(inspection.theme, null, 2),\n  `\\`\\`\\``,\n  ``,\n  `## Pagefind search`,\n  `- search element present: ${inspection.pagefind.searchEl}`,\n  ``,\n  `## Broken images`,\n  inspection.brokenImages.length\n    ? inspection.brokenImages.map((s) => `- ${s}`).join(\"\\n\")\n    : `(none)`,\n  ``,\n  ...errorBlock,\n].join(\"\\n\");\n\nawait writeFile(join(outDir, \"report.md\"), report);\nconsole.log(`  Saved: ${outDir}/report.md`);\n\n// Any page error is a hard fail — makes this usable as a quick gate.\nlet exitCode = 0;\nif (httpStatus !== 200) {\n  console.error(`\\n  FAIL  HTTP ${httpStatus} (expected 200)`);\n  exitCode = 1;\n}\nif (pageErrors.length > 0) {\n  console.error(`\\n  FAIL  ${pageErrors.length} page error(s)`);\n  exitCode = 1;\n}\nif (!inspection.main.found) {\n  console.error(`\\n  FAIL  <main> element not found`);\n  exitCode = 1;\n}\nif (inspection.brokenImages.length > 0) {\n  console.error(`\\n  FAIL  ${inspection.brokenImages.length} broken image(s)`);\n  exitCode = 1;\n}\n\n// ── Teardown ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\nif (!KEEP) {\n  await browser.close();\n  server.stop(true);\n  console.log(exitCode === 0 ? `\\n  OK` : `\\n  FAILED`);\n  process.exit(exitCode);\n} else {\n  console.log(`\\n  (keeping browser open; Ctrl+C to exit)`);\n  await new Promise(() => {});\n}\n",
  "file_path": "/mnt/c/Users/Cybersader/Documents/1 Projects, Workspaces/portaconv/docs/scripts/visual.mjs"
}

## Commit cadence

|---|---|---|

| 3 | **Playwright visual harness** | `docs/scripts/visual.mjs`, playwright dev-dep bump in `docs/package.json` |

  "content": "//! Shared in-memory model — adapter-agnostic.\n//!\n//! Both `Conversation` and `Message` carry a\n//! `extensions: serde_json::Value` bag for tool-specific fields the\n//! core schema doesn't promote.\n\nuse std::path::PathBuf;\n\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse serde_json::Value;\n\n/// A normalized conversation in shared-model form.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Conversation {\n    pub id: String,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub title: Option<String>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub cwd: Option<PathBuf>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub started_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,\n    pub messages: Vec<Message>,\n    #[serde(default, skip_serializing_if = \"Value::is_null\")]\n    pub extensions: Value,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Message {\n    pub role: Role,\n    pub content: Vec<ContentBlock>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub timestamp: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,\n    #[serde(default, skip_serializing_if = \"Value::is_null\")]\n    pub extensions: Value,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n#[serde(rename_all = \"lowercase\")]\npub enum Role {\n    User,\n    Assistant,\n    System,\n    Tool,\n}\n\n/// Anthropic-style content blocks. `thinking` is preserved as a distinct\n/// variant even though the default renderer collapses it — lossless on\n/// input is the whole point.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n#[serde(tag = \"type\", rename_all = \"snake_case\")]\npub enum ContentBlock {\n    Text {\n        text: String,\n    },\n    ToolUse {\n        id: String,\n        name: String,\n        input: Value,\n    },\n    ToolResult {\n        tool_use_id: String,\n        output: String,\n        #[serde(default)]\n        is_error: bool,\n    },\n    Thinking {\n        text: String,\n    },\n    /// Catch-all for blocks the v0.1 adapter doesn't promote to first class\n    /// (image / document / unknown). The raw JSON is preserved so a future\n    /// adapter version can upgrade without a data migration.\n    Unknown {\n        raw: Value,\n    },\n}\n\nimpl ContentBlock {\n    pub fn text(s: impl Into<String>) -> Self {\n        Self::Text { text: s.into() }\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    #[test]\n    fn roundtrip_minimal_conversation() {\n        let c = Conversation {\n            id: \"abc\".into(),\n            title: None,\n            cwd: None,\n            started_at: None,\n            messages: vec![Message {\n                role: Role::User,\n                content: vec![ContentBlock::text(\"hi\")],\n                timestamp: None,\n                extensions: Value::Null,\n            }],\n            extensions: Value::Null,\n        };\n        let s = serde_json::to_string(&c).unwrap();\n        let back: Conversation = serde_json::from_str(&s).unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(back.id, \"abc\");\n        assert_eq!(back.messages.len(), 1);\n        assert!(matches!(back.messages[0].role, Role::User));\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn content_block_tag_is_snake_case_type() {\n        let b = ContentBlock::ToolUse {\n            id: \"t1\".into(),\n            name: \"Read\".into(),\n            input: serde_json::json!({\"file_path\": \"/tmp/x\"}),\n        };\n        let s = serde_json::to_string(&b).unwrap();\n        assert!(s.contains(\"\\\"type\\\":\\\"tool_use\\\"\"));\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn unknown_block_preserves_raw() {\n        let raw = serde_json::json!({\"type\": \"image\", \"source\": \"…\"});\n        let block: ContentBlock = serde_json::from_value(raw.clone()).unwrap_or(\n            ContentBlock::Unknown { raw: raw.clone() },\n        );\n        if let ContentBlock::Unknown { raw: r } = block {\n            assert_eq!(r, raw);\n        }\n    }\n}\n",

  "content": "//! Adapter trait — one implementation per agent CLI whose storage we\n//! normalize. v0.1 ships only the Claude Code adapter; OpenCode / Cursor\n//! / Aider / continue.dev are separate PRs that land after this trait\n//! has survived contact with reality.\n\nuse std::path::PathBuf;\n\nuse anyhow::Result;\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\n\nuse crate::model::Conversation;\n\npub mod claude_code;\n\n/// Lightweight session entry returned by `list()`. Cheap to produce —\n/// the adapter does not parse the full message stream for listings.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct SessionMeta {\n    pub id: String,\n    pub tool: &'static str,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub title: Option<String>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub cwd: Option<PathBuf>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub started_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub updated_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,\n    pub message_count: usize,\n    /// Path to the on-disk backing file. Kept so `load(id)` can find it\n    /// without re-walking the corpus.\n    pub source_path: PathBuf,\n}\n\n/// Scope for `list()` calls. v0.1 doesn't wire portagenty integration —\n/// the field is present so the trait shape is stable when the pa shim\n/// lands in a later PR.\n#[derive(Debug, Default, Clone)]\npub struct WorkspaceScope {\n    pub project_paths: Vec<PathBuf>,\n    pub since: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,\n}\n\npub trait ConvoAdapter: Send + Sync {\n    fn id(&self) -> &'static str;\n    fn detect(&self) -> bool;\n    fn list(&self, scope: Option<&WorkspaceScope>) -> Result<Vec<SessionMeta>>;\n    fn load(&self, id: &str) -> Result<Conversation>;\n}\n",
