**tool call:** `Write`

```json
{
  "content": "//! Claude Code adapter.\n//!\n//! Reads `~/.claude/projects/*/*.jsonl` (and nested session dirs). Each\n//! line is one JSON record; records with `type ∈ {user, assistant}` carry\n//! conversational content, the rest are metadata. See\n//! `docs/src/content/docs/reference/adapter-claude-code.md` for the\n//! full record-type contract — this file is the implementation of it.\n\nuse std::fs;\nuse std::fs::File;\nuse std::io::{BufRead, BufReader};\nuse std::path::{Path, PathBuf};\n\nuse anyhow::{anyhow, Context, Result};\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse serde_json::Value;\n\nuse super::{ConvoAdapter, SessionMeta, WorkspaceScope};\nuse crate::model::{ContentBlock, Conversation, Message, Role};\n\n/// Storage root for Claude Code. Overridable via env for tests.\nfn projects_root() -> Option<PathBuf> {\n    if let Ok(p) = std::env::var(\"PORTACONV_CLAUDE_ROOT\") {\n        return Some(PathBuf::from(p));\n    }\n    dirs::home_dir().map(|h| h.join(\".claude\").join(\"projects\"))\n}\n\npub struct ClaudeCode;\n\nimpl ConvoAdapter for ClaudeCode {\n    fn id(&self) -> &'static str {\n        \"claude-code\"\n    }\n\n    fn detect(&self) -> bool {\n        projects_root().map(|p| p.is_dir()).unwrap_or(false)\n    }\n\n    fn list(&self, scope: Option<&WorkspaceScope>) -> Result<Vec<SessionMeta>> {\n        let root = projects_root().ok_or_else(|| anyhow!(\"no home dir\"))?;\n        if !root.is_dir() {\n            return Ok(Vec::new());\n        }\n\n        let mut out: Vec<SessionMeta> = Vec::new();\n        for file in walk_jsonls(&root)? {\n            if is_subagent_file(&file) {\n                continue;\n            }\n            // Per the research spike a single file can hold multiple\n            // sessionIds (/compact rewrites the continuation under a new\n            // id but appends to the same file). list() surfaces every\n            // distinct sessionId — matches Claude's /resume mental model.\n            for meta in scan_file(&file)?.into_iter() {\n                if let Some(s) = scope {\n                    if !scope_matches(&meta, s) {\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                }\n                out.push(meta);\n            }\n        }\n        out.sort_by(|a, b| b.updated_at.cmp(&a.updated_at));\n        Ok(out)\n    }\n\n    fn load(&self, id: &str) -> Result<Conversation> {\n        let root = projects_root().ok_or_else(|| anyhow!(\"no home dir\"))?;\n        for file in walk_jsonls(&root)? {\n            if is_subagent_file(&file) {\n                continue;\n            }\n            if file_contains_session(&file, id)? {\n                return parse_session(&file, id);\n            }\n        }\n        Err(anyhow!(\"session {id} not found under {}\", root.display()))\n    }\n}\n\nfn walk_jsonls(root: &Path) -> Result<Vec<PathBuf>> {\n    let mut acc = Vec::new();\n    walk(root, &mut acc)?;\n    Ok(acc)\n}\n\nfn walk(dir: &Path, acc: &mut Vec<PathBuf>) -> Result<()> {\n    let rd = match fs::read_dir(dir) {\n        Ok(r) => r,\n        Err(_) => return Ok(()), // unreadable subtree isn't fatal\n    };\n    for entry in rd.flatten() {\n        let p = entry.path();\n        if p.is_dir() {\n            walk(&p, acc)?;\n        } else if p.extension().and_then(|e| e.to_str()) == Some(\"jsonl\") {\n            acc.push(p);\n        }\n    }\n    Ok(())\n}\n\nfn is_subagent_file(p: &Path) -> bool {\n    // New shape: any ancestor dir named `subagents`.\n    let in_subagents_dir = p\n        .components()\n        .any(|c| c.as_os_str() == \"subagents\");\n    if in_subagents_dir {\n        return true;\n    }\n    // Old shape: project-root `agent-<hash>.jsonl` files (Claude ≤ 2.0.x\n    // wrote subagent sessions here). Per the adapter notes §4.\n    p.file_name()\n        .and_then(|n| n.to_str())\n        .map(|n| n.starts_with(\"agent-\") && n.ends_with(\".jsonl\"))\n        .unwrap_or(false)\n}\n\nfn scope_matches(meta: &SessionMeta, scope: &WorkspaceScope) -> bool {\n    if let Some(since) = scope.since {\n        let last = meta.updated_at.or(meta.started_at);\n        if last.map(|t| t < since).unwrap_or(true) {\n            return false;\n        }\n    }\n    if !scope.project_paths.is_empty() {\n        let Some(cwd) = meta.cwd.as_ref() else {\n            return false;\n        };\n        let matched = scope\n            .project_paths\n            .iter()\n            .any(|p| cwd.starts_with(p) || cwd == p);\n        if !matched {\n            return false;\n        }\n    }\n    true\n}\n\n/// First pass: cheap scan for SessionMeta. Does not parse content\n/// bodies — only touches a few fields per line.\nfn scan_file(path: &Path) -> Result<Vec<SessionMeta>> {\n    let f =\n        File::open(path).with_context(|| format!(\"open {}\", path.display()))?;\n    let rdr = BufReader::new(f);\n\n    // One entry per distinct sessionId seen in the file.\n    use std::collections::BTreeMap;\n    struct Acc {\n        cwd: Option<PathBuf>,\n        first_ts: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,\n        last_ts: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,\n        msg_count: usize,\n        title: Option<String>,\n    }\n    let mut per_session: BTreeMap<String, Acc> = BTreeMap::new();\n\n    for line in rdr.lines() {\n        let Ok(line) = line else { continue };\n        if line.is_empty() {\n            continue;\n        }\n        let Ok(v) = serde_json::from_str::<Value>(&line) else {\n            continue;\n        };\n\n        let Some(sid) = v.get(\"sessionId\").and_then(|s| s.as_str()) else {\n            continue;\n        };\n        let acc = per_session.entry(sid.to_string()).or_insert(Acc {\n            cwd: None,\n            first_ts: None,\n            last_ts: None,\n            msg_count: 0,\n            title: None,\n        });\n\n        if acc.cwd.is_none() {\n            if let Some(cwd) = v.get(\"cwd\").and_then(|s| s.as_str()) {\n                acc.cwd = Some(PathBuf::from(cwd));\n            }\n        }\n\n        if let Some(ts) = v.get(\"timestamp\").and_then(|s| s.as_str()) {\n            if let Ok(parsed) = DateTime::parse_from_rfc3339(ts) {\n                let parsed = parsed.with_timezone(&Utc);\n                acc.first_ts = Some(acc.first_ts.map_or(parsed, |e| e.min(parsed)));\n                acc.last_ts = Some(acc.last_ts.map_or(parsed, |e| e.max(parsed)));\n            }\n        }\n\n        let ty = v.get(\"type\").and_then(|s| s.as_str()).unwrap_or(\"\");\n        if matches!(ty, \"user\" | \"assistant\") {\n            acc.msg_count += 1;\n            if acc.title.is_none() && ty == \"user\" {\n                // Title derived from the first user message's text. The\n                // research spike saw message.content either as an array\n                // of blocks or (older Claude) as a bare string.\n                acc.title = extract_title(&v);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    Ok(per_session\n        .into_iter()\n        .map(|(id, acc)| SessionMeta {\n            id,\n            tool: \"claude-code\",\n            title: acc.title,\n            cwd: acc.cwd,\n            started_at: acc.first_ts,\n            updated_at: acc.last_ts,\n            message_count: acc.msg_count,\n            source_path: path.to_path_buf(),\n        })\n        .collect())\n}\n\nfn extract_title(v: &Value) -> Option<String> {\n    let content = v.pointer(\"/message/content\")?;\n    let text = match content {\n        Value::String(s) => s.clone(),\n        Value::Array(arr) => arr\n            .iter()\n            .find_map(|b| {\n                if b.get(\"type\").and_then(|t| t.as_str()) == Some(\"text\") {\n                    b.get(\"text\").and_then(|t| t.as_str()).map(str::to_string)\n                } else {\n                    None\n                }\n            })\n            .unwrap_or_default(),\n        _ => return None,\n    };\n    let first_line = text.lines().next().unwrap_or_default().trim();\n    if first_line.is_empty() {\n        None\n    } else {\n        // Keep it short. The renderer can show more if needed.\n        Some(first_line.chars().take(120).collect())\n    }\n}\n\nfn file_contains_session(path: &Path, id: &str) -> Result<bool> {\n    let f = File::open(path)?;\n    let rdr = BufReader::new(f);\n    let needle = format!(\"\\\"sessionId\\\":\\\"{id}\\\"\");\n    for line in rdr.lines() {\n        let Ok(line) = line else { continue };\n        // Substring check is sufficient — sessionId values are 36-char\n        // UUIDs so collisions against unrelated substrings are not a\n        // practical concern. Correct-parse happens in parse_session().\n        if line.contains(&needle) {\n            return Ok(true);\n        }\n    }\n    Ok(false)\n}\n\n/// Second pass: full parse, filtered to the requested sessionId.\nfn parse_session(path: &Path, session_id: &str) -> Result<Conversation> {\n    let f =\n        File::open(path).with_context(|| format!(\"open {}\", path.display()))?;\n    let rdr = BufReader::new(f);\n\n    let mut messages: Vec<Message> = Vec::new();\n    let mut cwd: Option<PathBuf> = None;\n    let mut started_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>> = None;\n    let mut title: Option<String> = None;\n    let mut system_events: Vec<Value> = Vec::new();\n    let mut unknown_records: Vec<Value> = Vec::new();\n\n    for line in rdr.lines() {\n        let Ok(line) = line else { continue };\n        if line.is_empty() {\n            continue;\n        }\n        let Ok(v) = serde_json::from_str::<Value>(&line) else {\n            continue;\n        };\n        if v.get(\"sessionId\").and_then(|s| s.as_str()) != Some(session_id) {\n            continue;\n        }\n\n        if cwd.is_none() {\n            if let Some(c) = v.get(\"cwd\").and_then(|s| s.as_str()) {\n                cwd = Some(PathBuf::from(c));\n            }\n        }\n\n        let ty = v.get(\"type\").and_then(|s| s.as_str()).unwrap_or(\"\");\n        let ts = v.get(\"timestamp\").and_then(|s| s.as_str()).and_then(|s| {\n            DateTime::parse_from_rfc3339(s).ok().map(|t| t.with_timezone(&Utc))\n        });\n        if started_at.is_none() {\n            started_at = ts;\n        }\n\n        match ty {\n            \"user\" | \"assistant\" => {\n                let role = if ty == \"user\" { Role::User } else { Role::Assistant };\n                let content = decode_content(&v);\n                if role == Role::User && title.is_none() {\n                    title = extract_title(&v);\n                }\n                messages.push(Message {\n                    role,\n                    content,\n                    timestamp: ts,\n                    extensions: keep_message_extensions(&v),\n                });\n            }\n            \"system\" => {\n                system_events.push(v.clone());\n            }\n            // Skipped per adapter notes §3.\n            \"file-history-snapshot\" | \"progress\" | \"queue-operation\" => {}\n            _ => {\n                // Unknown — surface in extensions per the resilience rule.\n                unknown_records.push(v.clone());\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    if messages.is_empty() && system_events.is_empty() {\n        return Err(anyhow!(\n            \"no records in {} matched sessionId {session_id}\",\n            path.display()\n        ));\n    }\n\n    let mut ext = serde_json::Map::new();\n    if !system_events.is_empty() {\n        ext.insert(\"system_events\".into(), Value::Array(system_events));\n    }\n    if !unknown_records.is_empty() {\n        ext.insert(\n            \"unknown_records\".into(),\n            Value::Array(unknown_records),\n        );\n    }\n    let extensions = if ext.is_empty() {\n        Value::Null\n    } else {\n        Value::Object(ext)\n    };\n\n    Ok(Conversation {\n        id: session_id.to_string(),\n        title,\n        cwd,\n        started_at,\n        messages,\n        extensions,\n    })\n}\n\n/// Pull the in-record fields the adapter promotes to per-message\n/// extensions. Keep it small — anything not used downstream stays out\n/// of the shared model's surface.\nfn keep_message_extensions(v: &Value) -> Value {\n    let Some(obj) = v.as_object() else {\n        return Value::Null;\n    };\n    let mut out = serde_json::Map::new();\n    for k in [\n        \"uuid\",\n        \"parentUuid\",\n        \"requestId\",\n        \"isSidechain\",\n        \"isMeta\",\n        \"isApiErrorMessage\",\n        \"isCompactSummary\",\n        \"isVisibleInTranscriptOnly\",\n        \"slug\",\n        \"userType\",\n        \"gitBranch\",\n        \"version\",\n        \"permissionMode\",\n        \"thinkingMetadata\",\n        \"compactMetadata\",\n        \"logicalParentUuid\",\n    ] {\n        if let Some(val) = obj.get(k) {\n            out.insert(k.to_string(), val.clone());\n        }\n    }\n    if out.is_empty() {\n        Value::Null\n    } else {\n        Value::Object(out)\n    }\n}\n\nfn decode_content(v: &Value) -> Vec<ContentBlock> {\n    let content = match v.pointer(\"/message/content\") {\n        Some(c) => c,\n        None => return Vec::new(),\n    };\n    match content {\n        Value::String(s) => vec![ContentBlock::text(s.clone())],\n        Value::Array(arr) => arr.iter().map(decode_block).collect(),\n        _ => Vec::new(),\n    }\n}\n\nfn decode_block(b: &Value) -> ContentBlock {\n    let ty = b.get(\"type\").and_then(|s| s.as_str()).unwrap_or(\"\");\n    match ty {\n        \"text\" => ContentBlock::Text {\n            text: b.get(\"text\").and_then(|t| t.as_str()).unwrap_or(\"\").into(),\n        },\n        \"thinking\" => ContentBlock::Thinking {\n            text: b.get(\"thinking\").and_then(|t| t.as_str())\n                .or_else(|| b.get(\"text\").and_then(|t| t.as_str()))\n                .unwrap_or(\"\")\n                .into(),\n        },\n        \"tool_use\" => ContentBlock::ToolUse {\n            id: b.get(\"id\").and_then(|s| s.as_str()).unwrap_or(\"\").into(),\n            name: b.get(\"name\").and_then(|s| s.as_str()).unwrap_or(\"\").into(),\n            input: b.get(\"input\").cloned().unwrap_or(Value::Null),\n        },\n        \"tool_result\" => ContentBlock::ToolResult {\n            tool_use_id: b\n                .get(\"tool_use_id\")\n                .and_then(|s| s.as_str())\n                .unwrap_or(\"\")\n                .into(),\n            output: match b.get(\"content\") {\n                Some(Value::String(s)) => s.clone(),\n                Some(Value::Array(arr)) => arr\n                    .iter()\n                    .filter_map(|x| x.get(\"text\").and_then(|t| t.as_str()))\n                    .collect::<Vec<_>>()\n                    .join(\"\\n\"),\n                _ => String::new(),\n            },\n            is_error: b\n                .get(\"is_error\")\n                .and_then(|x| x.as_bool())\n                .unwrap_or(false),\n        },\n        _ => ContentBlock::Unknown { raw: b.clone() },\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    #[test]\n    fn subagent_detection() {\n        assert!(is_subagent_file(Path::new(\n            \"/x/-mnt-…-proj/abc/subagents/agent-xyz.jsonl\"\n        )));\n        assert!(is_subagent_file(Path::new(\n            \"/x/-mnt-…-proj/agent-a1234.jsonl\"\n        )));\n        assert!(!is_subagent_file(Path::new(\n            \"/x/-mnt-…-proj/9decac91-1ead-4324.jsonl\"\n        )));\n    }\n}\n",
  "file_path": "/mnt/c/Users/Cybersader/Documents/1 Projects, Workspaces/portaconv/src/adapters/claude_code.rs"
}

{
  "content": "//! CLI argument parsing. v0.1 surface: `list`, `dump`, `mcp serve`.\n//!\n//! Markdown rendering + --rewrite transforms are stubbed here but land\n//! as a follow-up commit — this file's scope is the argument shape and\n//! the `list` / `dump --format json` execution paths.\n\nuse std::io::{self, Write};\n\nuse anyhow::{anyhow, Context, Result};\nuse clap::{Parser, Subcommand, ValueEnum};\n\nuse crate::adapters::{ClaudeCode, ConvoAdapter, WorkspaceScope};\n\n#[derive(Parser, Debug)]\n#[command(name = \"pconv\", version, about = \"Terminal-native conversation extractor for agent CLIs\")]\npub struct Cli {\n    #[command(subcommand)]\n    pub command: Command,\n}\n\n#[derive(Subcommand, Debug)]\npub enum Command {\n    /// List conversations discoverable on this machine.\n    List(ListArgs),\n    /// Dump one session to stdout.\n    Dump(DumpArgs),\n    /// MCP-related subcommands.\n    Mcp {\n        #[command(subcommand)]\n        sub: McpCommand,\n    },\n}\n\n#[derive(clap::Args, Debug)]\npub struct ListArgs {\n    /// Output format.\n    #[arg(long, value_enum, default_value_t = ListFormat::Table)]\n    pub format: ListFormat,\n    /// Hide sessions with fewer than this many messages.\n    #[arg(long, default_value_t = 1)]\n    pub min_messages: usize,\n}\n\n#[derive(clap::Args, Debug)]\npub struct DumpArgs {\n    /// Session ID (UUID).\n    pub session_id: String,\n    /// Output format.\n    #[arg(long, value_enum, default_value_t = DumpFormat::Json)]\n    pub format: DumpFormat,\n}\n\n#[derive(Subcommand, Debug)]\npub enum McpCommand {\n    /// Start the stdio MCP server (not implemented in v0.0.2).\n    Serve,\n}\n\n#[derive(Copy, Clone, Debug, ValueEnum)]\npub enum ListFormat {\n    Table,\n    Json,\n}\n\n#[derive(Copy, Clone, Debug, ValueEnum)]\npub enum DumpFormat {\n    Json,\n    // Markdown — lands with the renderer commit.\n}\n\npub fn run(cli: Cli) -> Result<()> {\n    match cli.command {\n        Command::List(args) => run_list(args),\n        Command::Dump(args) => run_dump(args),\n        Command::Mcp { sub: McpCommand::Serve } => Err(anyhow!(\n            \"pconv mcp serve is not implemented yet — tracked for a follow-up commit\"\n        )),\n    }\n}\n\nfn run_list(args: ListArgs) -> Result<()> {\n    let adapter = ClaudeCode;\n    if !adapter.detect() {\n        return Err(anyhow!(\n            \"Claude Code storage not found. Expected ~/.claude/projects/ (or set PORTACONV_CLAUDE_ROOT)\"\n        ));\n    }\n    let scope = WorkspaceScope::default();\n    let mut sessions = adapter\n        .list(Some(&scope))\n        .context(\"listing Claude Code sessions\")?;\n    sessions.retain(|s| s.message_count >= args.min_messages);\n\n    let out = io::stdout();\n    let mut out = out.lock();\n    match args.format {\n        ListFormat::Json => {\n            serde_json::to_writer_pretty(&mut out, &sessions)?;\n            writeln!(out)?;\n        }\n        ListFormat::Table => {\n            writeln!(\n                out,\n                \"{:<36}  {:>5}  {:<20}  {}\",\n                \"session-id\", \"msgs\", \"updated\", \"title\"\n            )?;\n            writeln!(out, \"{}\", \"-\".repeat(100))?;\n            for s in &sessions {\n                let updated = s\n                    .updated_at\n                    .map(|t| t.format(\"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M\").to_string())\n                    .unwrap_or_else(|| \"-\".into());\n                let title = s\n                    .title\n                    .as_deref()\n                    .unwrap_or(\"(untitled)\");\n                let truncated: String = title.chars().take(60).collect();\n                writeln!(\n                    out,\n                    \"{:<36}  {:>5}  {:<20}  {}\",\n                    s.id, s.message_count, updated, truncated\n                )?;\n            }\n            writeln!(out, \"\\n{} session(s)\", sessions.len())?;\n        }\n    }\n    Ok(())\n}\n\nfn run_dump(args: DumpArgs) -> Result<()> {\n    let adapter = ClaudeCode;\n    if !adapter.detect() {\n        return Err(anyhow!(\n            \"Claude Code storage not found. Expected ~/.claude/projects/ (or set PORTACONV_CLAUDE_ROOT)\"\n        ));\n    }\n    let conv = adapter.load(&args.session_id)?;\n    let out = io::stdout();\n    let mut out = out.lock();\n    match args.format {\n        DumpFormat::Json => {\n            serde_json::to_writer_pretty(&mut out, &conv)?;\n            writeln!(out)?;\n        }\n    }\n    Ok(())\n}\n",
  "file_path": "/mnt/c/Users/Cybersader/Documents/1 Projects, Workspaces/portaconv/src/cli.rs"
}

Same DOM inspection as\n// docs/scripts/visual.mjs, different base URL + no local static server.\n\nimport { mkdirSync } from \"node:fs\";\nimport { writeFile } from \"node:fs/promises\";\nimport { join } from \"node:path\";\nimport { chromium } from \"/mnt/c/Users/Cybersader/Documents/1 Projects, Workspaces/portaconv/docs/node_modules/playwright/index.mjs\";\n\nconst BASE = \"https://cybersader.github.io/portaconv\";\nconst PAGES = [\n  { path: \"/\", label: \"home\" },\n  { path: \"/getting-started/installation/\", label: \"installation\" },\n  { path: \"/concepts/\", label: \"concepts\" },\n  { path: \"/reference/commands/\", label: \"commands\" },\n  { path: \"/reference/adapter-claude-code/\", label: \"adapter-claude-code\" },\n];\nconst VIEWPORT = { width: 1440, height: 900 }; // desktop — closer to typical review\n\nconst outDir = `/tmp/pconv-live-${Date.now()}`;\nmkdirSync(outDir, { recursive: true });\n\nconst browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });\nconst context = await browser.newContext({ viewport: VIEWPORT });\n\nlet failures = 0;\nconst summary = [];\n\nfor (const { path, label } of PAGES) {\n  const page = await context.newPage();\n  const consoleLogs = [];\n  const pageErrors = [];\n  page.on(\"console\", (msg) => consoleLogs.push({ type: msg.type(), text: msg.text() }));\n  page.on(\"pageerror\", (err) => pageErrors.push(err.message));\n\n  const url = `${BASE}${path}`;\n  const res = await page.goto(url, { waitUntil: \"networkidle\", timeout: 30_000 });\n  const status = res ? res.status() : 0;\n\n  const insp = await page.evaluate(() => ({\n    title: document.title,\n    h1: document.querySelector(\"main h1\")?.textContent?.trim() ?? null,\n    h2Count: document.querySelectorAll(\"main h2\").length,\n    tableCount: document.querySelectorAll(\"main table\").length,\n    codeBlocks: document.querySelectorAll(\"main pre > code\").length,\n    sidebarLinks: document.querySelectorAll(\".sidebar a[href]\").length,\n    slColorAccent: getComputedStyle(document.documentElement)\n      .getPropertyValue(\"--sl-color-accent\").trim(),\n    pagefindPresent: !!document.querySelector(\n      '[data-pagefind-search], #starlight__search, [data-pagefind-ui]',\n    ),\n    brokenImages: Array.from(document.images)\n      .filter((i) => i.complete && i.naturalWidth === 0)\n      .map((i) => i.src),\n  }));\n\n  await page.screenshot({ path: join(outDir, `${label}.png`), fullPage: true });\n\n  const ok =\n    status === 200 &&\n    pageErrors.length === 0 &&\n    insp.h1 !== null &&\n    insp.brokenImages.length === 0;\n  if (!ok) failures++;\n\n  summary.push({\n    path,\n    status,\n    h1: insp.h1,\n    h2Count: insp.h2Count,\n    tableCount: insp.tableCount,\n    codeBlocks: insp.codeBlocks,\n    sidebarLinks: insp.sidebarLinks,\n    theme: insp.slColorAccent,\n    pagefind: insp.pagefindPresent,\n    brokenImages: insp.brokenImages.length,\n    pageErrors: pageErrors.length,\n    consoleCount: consoleLogs.length,\n    consoleFirst: consoleLogs.slice(0, 3).map((l) => `[${l.type}] ${l.text}`),\n    ok,\n  });\n  await page.close();\n}\n\nawait writeFile(join(outDir, \"report.json\"), JSON.stringify(summary, null, 2));\n\nconsole.log(`output dir: ${outDir}`);\nconsole.log(\"\");\nconsole.log(\"path\".padEnd(40), \"status\", \"h1\".padEnd(32), \"h2\", \"tables\", \"sidebar\", \"ok\");\nfor (const r of summary) {\n  console.log(\n    r.path.padEnd(40),\n    String(r.status).padEnd(6),\n    (r.h1 ?? \"\").slice(0, 30).padEnd(32),\n    String(r.h2Count).padEnd(2),\n    String(r.tableCount).padEnd(6),\n    String(r.sidebarLinks).padEnd(7),\n    r.ok ? \"OK\" : \"FAIL\",\n  );\n}\nconsole.log(\"\");\nconsole.log(failures === 0 ? \"ALL GREEN\" : `${failures} FAILED`);\n\nawait browser.close();\nprocess.exit(failures === 0 ? 0 : 1);\n",
  "file_path": "/tmp/visual-live.mjs"
}

## User

**tool result:**

```

## Assistant

**tool call:** `Write`

```json
{
  "content": "//! Paste-ready markdown renderer.\n//!\n//! Goal: when the output is pasted into a fresh agent session, the\n//! agent picks up the substantive context. Tool-call *state* doesn't\n//! survive the paste — that's by design per the design-decisions doc\n//! (the tool-call args are re-runnable against the current filesystem\n//! anyway, so we preserve the intent, not the replay).\n//!\n//! Defaults: thinking blocks collapsed, tool results truncated to a\n//! short preview. Both are overridable via `MarkdownOptions` so a\n//! user pasting between long-context agents can keep the lot.\n\nuse std::fmt::Write;\n\nuse crate::model::{ContentBlock, Conversation, Message, Role};\n\n/// Knobs for the renderer. Defaults lean paste-ergonomic — small\n/// output that still reads like a conversation.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MarkdownOptions {\n    /// Include `ContentBlock::Thinking` blocks verbatim. Default off —\n    /// thinking is internal reasoning, rarely worth pasting back.\n    pub include_thinking: bool,\n    /// Emit full tool-result bodies. Default off — results are capped\n    /// at `tool_result_preview_chars` and get a truncation marker.\n    pub full_results: bool,\n    /// Preview cap for `tool_result` when `full_results` is false.\n    pub tool_result_preview_chars: usize,\n    /// Include `system_events` from conversation-level extensions as\n    /// a trailing block. Default off — it's noise for paste workflows.\n    pub include_system_events: bool,\n}\n\nimpl Default for MarkdownOptions {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            include_thinking: false,\n            full_results: false,\n            tool_result_preview_chars: 600,\n            include_system_events: false,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\npub fn render_markdown(conv: &Conversation, opts: &MarkdownOptions) -> String {\n    let mut out = String::new();\n\n    // Header — keep small; the conversation body is the product.\n    let title = conv.title.as_deref().unwrap_or(\"(untitled)\");\n    let _ = writeln!(out, \"# {title}\");\n    let _ = writeln!(out);\n    let _ = writeln!(out, \"- session: `{}`\", conv.id);\n    if let Some(cwd) = conv.cwd.as_ref() {\n        let _ = writeln!(out, \"- cwd: `{}`\", cwd.display());\n    }\n    if let Some(t) = conv.started_at {\n        let _ = writeln!(out, \"- started: {}\", t.format(\"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M UTC\"));\n    }\n    if let Some(branch) = conv\n        .messages\n        .first()\n        .and_then(|m| m.extensions.get(\"gitBranch\"))\n        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())\n        .filter(|s| !s.is_empty())\n    {\n        let _ = writeln!(out, \"- git branch: `{branch}`\");\n    }\n    let _ = writeln!(out);\n\n    for msg in &conv.messages {\n        render_message(&mut out, msg, opts);\n    }\n\n    if opts.include_system_events {\n        if let Some(events) = conv.extensions.get(\"system_events\").and_then(|v| v.as_array()) {\n            if !events.is_empty() {\n                let _ = writeln!(out, \"---\");\n                let _ = writeln!(out);\n                let _ = writeln!(out, \"## System events\");\n                let _ = writeln!(out);\n                for ev in events {\n                    let _ = writeln!(out, \"- `{ev}`\");\n                }\n                let _ = writeln!(out);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    out\n}\n\nfn render_message(out: &mut String, msg: &Message, opts: &MarkdownOptions) {\n    let heading = match msg.role {\n        Role::User => \"## User\",\n        Role::Assistant => \"## Assistant\",\n        Role::System => \"## System\",\n        Role::Tool => \"## Tool\",\n    };\n    let _ = writeln!(out, \"{heading}\");\n    let _ = writeln!(out);\n\n    for block in &msg.content {\n        render_block(out, block, opts);\n    }\n}\n\nfn render_block(out: &mut String, block: &ContentBlock, opts: &MarkdownOptions) {\n    match block {\n        ContentBlock::Text { text } => {\n            let _ = writeln!(out, \"{}\", text.trim_end());\n            let _ = writeln!(out);\n        }\n        ContentBlock::Thinking { text } => {\n            if opts.include_thinking {\n                let _ = writeln!(out, \"> _thinking:_\");\n                for line in text.lines() {\n                    let _ = writeln!(out, \"> {line}\");\n                }\n                let _ = writeln!(out);\n            }\n            // If skipped, emit nothing — a placeholder would clutter\n            // more than a missing block signals.\n        }\n        ContentBlock::ToolUse { id: _, name, input } => {\n            let _ = writeln!(out, \"**tool call:** `{name}`\");\n            let _ = writeln!(out);\n            let _ = writeln!(out, \"```json\");\n            // Pretty-print the input — makes paste-readable, and agents\n            // re-parse JSON reliably either way.\n            let rendered =\n                serde_json::to_string_pretty(input).unwrap_or_else(|_| input.to_string());\n            let _ = writeln!(out, \"{rendered}\");\n            let _ = writeln!(out, \"```\");\n            let _ = writeln!(out);\n        }\n        ContentBlock::ToolResult {\n            tool_use_id: _,\n            output,\n            is_error,\n        } => {\n            let label = if *is_error { \"tool result (error)\" } else { \"tool result\" };\n            let _ = writeln!(out, \"**{label}:**\");\n            let _ = writeln!(out);\n            let body = if opts.full_results || output.chars().count() <= opts.tool_result_preview_chars {\n                output.clone()\n            } else {\n                let truncated: String =\n                    output.chars().take(opts.tool_result_preview_chars).collect();\n                let dropped = output.chars().count() - opts.tool_result_preview_chars;\n                format!(\"{truncated}\\n… ({dropped} more chars truncated; --full-results to expand)\")\n            };\n            let _ = writeln!(out, \"```\");\n            let _ = writeln!(out, \"{}\", body.trim_end_matches('\\n'));\n            let _ = writeln!(out, \"```\");\n            let _ = writeln!(out);\n        }\n        ContentBlock::Unknown { raw } => {\n            let _ = writeln!(out, \"<!-- unknown content block preserved in extensions -->\");\n            let _ = writeln!(\n                out,\n                \"_unknown block:_ `{}`\",\n                raw.get(\"type\")\n                    .and_then(|t| t.as_str())\n                    .unwrap_or(\"?\")\n            );\n            let _ = writeln!(out);\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use crate::model::{ContentBlock, Conversation, Message, Role};\n    use serde_json::json;\n\n    fn sample() -> Conversation {\n        Conversation {\n            id: \"aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-000000000001\".into(),\n            title: Some(\"Hello world — please read README.md\".into()),\n            cwd:       content: vec![ContentBlock::text(\"Hello world — please read README.md\")],\n                    timestamp: None,\n                    extensions: json!({\"gitBranch\": \"main\", \"version\": \"2.1.51\"}),\n                },\n                Message {\n                    role: Role::Assistant,\n                    content: vec![\n                        ContentBlock::Thinking {\n \"/test/workspace/sample/README.md\"}),\n                        },\n                    ],\n                    timestamp: None,\n                    extensions: serde_json::Value::Null,\n {
  "content": "//! Opt-in content transforms applied to a loaded `Conversation`.\n//!\n//! v0.1 ships one: OS-path rewriting. This exists because Claude Code\n//! conversation JSONLs carry absolute filesystem paths from the\n//! authoring OS inside `cwd` fields, tool-call args, and prose — which\n//! means a WSL-authored session pastes badly into a Windows-launched\n//! agent (and vice versa). The spike measured 464/489 lines of one\n//! Windows-encoded session still carrying `/mnt/c/…` references.\n\npub mod paths;\n\npub use paths::{apply_path_rewrite, PathRewrite};\n",
  "file_path": "/mnt/c/Users/Cybersader/Documents/1 Projects, Workspaces/portaconv/src/transform/mod.rs"

## User

## Assistant

**tool call:** `Write`

```json
{
  "content": "//! OS-path rewriting inside conversation content.\n//!\n//! Scope (per adapter notes §7 Q#3):\n//!   - `ContentBlock::Text.text`        — prose written by user/assistant\n//!   - `ContentBlock::ToolUse.input`    — tool-call arguments (strings\n//!                                        inside the JSON only)\n//!   - `ContentBlock::ToolResult.output` — result bodies may carry paths\n//!\n//! NOT touched:\n//!   - `Conversation.cwd`     — metadata about the authoring environment\n//!   - `Message.extensions`   — adapter-preserved raw fields\n//!   - `ContentBlock::ToolUse.id` / `tool_use_id` — opaque handles\n//!   - `ContentBlock::Thinking` — reasoning trace, left verbatim\n//!\n//! Patterns are deliberately conservative: they match well-formed\n//! absolute paths and leave ambiguous cases alone. A user relying on\n//! the transform for correctness (vs convenience) should review the\n//! diff before pasting.\n\nuse std::sync::OnceLock;\n\nuse regex::{Captures, Regex};\nuse serde_json::Value;\n\nuse crate::model::{ContentBlock, Conversation};\n\n#[derive(Copy, Clone, Debug, PartialEq, Eq)]\npub enum PathRewrite {\n    /// `/mnt/c/…` → `C:\\…`. Only the WSL `/mnt/<letter>/…` form is\n    /// rewritten; bare `/home/user/…` stays untouched.\n    WslToWin,\n    /// `C:\\…` or `C:/…` → `/mnt/c/…`. Drive letters get lowercased.\n    WinToWsl,\n    /// Replace any absolute path (WSL-style OR Windows-style) with the\n    /// literal placeholder `<path>`. Useful when the paths shouldn't\n    /// just be translated but erased — e.g. when pasting into a\n    /// context that has no local filesystem to resolve against.\n    Strip,\n}\n\npub fn apply_path_rewrite(conv: &mut Conversation, mode: PathRewrite) {\n    for msg in &mut conv.messages {\n        for block in &mut msg.content {\n            match block {\n                ContentBlock::Text { text } => *text = rewrite_str(text, mode),\n                ContentBlock::ToolUse { input, .. } => rewrite_json(input, mode),\n                ContentBlock::ToolResult { output, .. } => {\n                    *output = rewrite_str(output, mode);\n                }\n                ContentBlock::Thinking { .. } | ContentBlock::Unknown { .. } => {}\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn rewrite_json(value: &mut Value, mode: PathRewrite) {\n    match value {\n        Value::String(s) => *s = rewrite_str(s, mode),\n        Value::Array(a) => a.iter_mut().for_each(|v| rewrite_json(v, mode)),\n        Value::Object(o) => o.values_mut().for_each(|v| rewrite_json(v, mode)),\n        _ => {}\n    }\n}\n\nfn wsl_re() -> &'static Regex {\n    static RE: OnceLock<Regex> = OnceLock::new();\n    // /mnt/<letter>/<rest-until-whitespace-or-quote-or-backtick-or-paren>\n    //\n    // Permissive but bounded: stops at whitespace, quotes, or markdown\n    // boundary chars so we don't grab the rest of a sentence. Paths\n    // with spaces inside are rare in practice and get half-rewritten;\n    // users who need space-paths should review the diff.\n    RE.get_or_init(|| Regex::new(r\"(?P<pre>^|[\\s\\(\\[\\{\\\"'`])(?:/mnt/)(?P<letter>[a-z])(?P<rest>(?:/[^\\s\\)\\]\\}\\\"'`]*)*)\").unwrap())\n}\n\nfn win_re() -> &'static Regex {\n    static RE: OnceLock<Regex> = OnceLock::new();\n    // <drive>:\\<rest> or <drive>:/<rest>\n    RE.get_or_init(|| Regex::new(r\"(?P<pre>^|[\\s\\(\\[\\{\\\"'`])(?P<drive>[A-Za-z]):(?P<sep>[\\\\/])(?P<rest>[^\\s\\)\\]\\}\\\"'`]*)\").unwrap())\n}\n\nfn rewrite_str(s: &str, mode: PathRewrite) -> String {\n    match mode {\n        PathRewrite::WslToWin => wsl_re()\n            .replace_all(s, |caps: &Captures| {\n                let pre = caps.name(\"pre\").map_or(\"\", |m| m.as_str());\n                let letter = caps\n                    .name(\"letter\")\n                    .map_or(\"\", |m| m.as_str())\n                    .to_ascii_uppercase();\n                let rest = caps\n                    .name(\"rest\")\n                    .map_or(\"\", |m| m.as_str())\n                    .replace('/', \"\\\\\");\n                // \"/mnt/c\" followed by nothing → \"C:\" looks incomplete.\n                // Keep the rest (possibly empty) so \"/mnt/c\" → \"C:\".\n                format!(\"{pre}{letter}:{rest}\")\n            })\n            .into_owned(),\n        PathRewrite::WinToWsl => win_re()\n            .replace_all(s, |caps: &Captures| {\n                let pre = caps.name(\"pre\").map_or(\"\", |m| m.as_str());\n                let letter = caps\n                    .name(\"drive\")\n                    .map_or(\"\", |m| m.as_str())\n                    .to_ascii_lowercase();\n                let rest = caps\n                    .name(\"rest\")\n                    .map_or(\"\", |m| m.as_str())\n                    .replace('\\\\', \"/\");\n                format!(\"{pre}/mnt/{letter}/{rest}\")\n            })\n            .into_owned(),\n        PathRewrite::Strip => {\n            // Apply both patterns; the leading-context `pre` is preserved.\n            let stripped_wsl = wsl_re().replace_all(s, \"${pre}<path>\");\n            let stripped_both = win_re().replace_all(&stripped_wsl, \"${pre}<path>\");\n            stripped_both.into_owned()\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use serde_json::json;\n\n    #[test]\n    fn wsl_to_win_basic() {\n        let out = rewrite_str(\n            \"open /mnt/c/Users/alice/doc.md please\",\n            PathRewrite::WslToWin,\n        );\n        assert_eq!(out, \"open C:\\\\Users\\\\alice\\\\doc.md please\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn win_to_wsl_basic() {\n        let out = rewrite_str(\n            \"open Paths with spaces inside get\n    // truncated at the space — users who need space-paths should review\n    // the diff. The letter class is strictly [a-z] so `Cargo/mnt/foo`\n    // (no drive-letter meaning) won't match; only /mnt/ followed by a\n    // single lowercase letter followed by / or end-of-boundary does.\n    RE.get_or_init(|| {\n        Regex::new(r#\"/mnt/(?P<letter>[a-z])(?P<rest>(?:/[^\\s\\)\\]\\}\"'`]*)*)\"#).unwrap()\n    })\n}\n\nfn win_re() -> &'static Regex {\n    static RE: OnceLock<Regex> = OnceLock::new();\n    // <drive>:\\<rest> or <drive>:/<non-slash-rest>. The forward-slash\n    // branch excludes a second `/` to avoid matching URL schemes like\n    // `https://` (where `s:` otherwise looks like a drive letter).\n    RE.get_or_init(|| {\n        Regex::new(\n            r#\"\\b(?P<drive>[A-Za-z]):(?:\\\\(?P<bsrest>[^\\s\\)\\]\\}\"'`]*)|/(?P<fsrest>[^/\\s\\)\\]\\}\"'`][^\\s\\)\\]\\}\"'`]*))\"#,\n        )\n        .unwrap()\n    })\n}\n\nfn rewrite_str(s: &str, mode: PathRewrite) -> String {\n    match mode {\n        PathRewrite::WslToWin => wsl_re()\n            .replace_all(s, |caps: &Captures| {\n                let letter = caps\n                    .name(\"letter\")\n                    .map_or(\"\", |m| m.as_str())\n                    .to_ascii_uppercase();\n                let rest = caps\n                    .name(\"rest\")\n                    .map_or(\"\", |m| m.as_str())\n                    .replace('/', \"\\\\\");\n                // \"/mnt/c\" followed by nothing → \"C:\" (valid — drive root).\n                format!(\"{letter}:{rest}\")\n            })\n            .into_owned(),\n        PathRewrite::WinToWsl => win_re()\n            .replace_all(s, |caps: &Captures| {\n                let letter = caps\n                    .name(\"drive\")\n                    .map_or(\"\", |m| m.as_str())\n                    .to_ascii_lowercase();\n                let rest = caps\n                    .name(\"bsrest\")\n                    .or_else(|| caps.name(\"fsrest\"))\n                    .map_or(\"\", |m| m.as_str())\n                    .replace('\\\\', \"/\");\n                format!(\"/mnt/{letter}/{rest}\")\n            })\n            .into_owned(),\n        PathRewrite::Strip => {\n            let stripped_wsl = wsl_re().replace_all(s, \"<path>\");\n            let stripped_both = win_re().replace_all(&stripped_wsl, \"<path>\");\n            stripped_both.into_owned()\n        }\n    }\n}",

Skim these\nbefore the reference.\n\n## The three layers\n\n<div style=\"display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 0.5rem; margin: 1.5rem 0;\">\n  <div style=\"display: grid; grid-template-columns: 8rem 1fr; gap: 0.75rem; align-items: stretch;\">\n    <div style=\"background: var(--sl-color-blue-low); border: 2px solid var(--sl-color-blue); border-radius: 10px; padding: 0.5rem 0.75rem; display: flex; flex-direction: column; justify-content: center; text-align: center;\">\n      <div style=\"font-weight: 700; font-size: 0.9rem;\">Adapter</div>\n      <div style=\"font-size: 0.7rem; font-family: var(--sl-font-mono); opacity: 0.7;\">tool-specific</div>\n    </div>\n    <div style=\"padding: 0.4rem 0;\">\n      <div style=\"font-weight: 600; font-size: 0.9rem;\">Read and normalize one tool's on-disk shape</div>\n      <div style=\"font-size: 0.85rem; opacity: 0.8; margin-top: 0.2rem;\">v0.1 ships the Claude Code adapter. The trait is small — <code>detect</code>, <code>list</code>, <code>load(id)</code> — so future adapters (opencode, Cursor, Aider, continue.dev) can land one-at-a-time without reshaping the core.</div>\n    </div>\n  </div>\n  <div style=\"display: grid; grid-template-columns: 8rem 1fr; gap: 0.75rem; align-items: stretch;\">\n    <div style=\"background: var(--sl-color-accent-low); border: 2px solid var(--sl-color-accent); border-radius: 10px; padding: 0.5rem 0.75rem; display: flex; flex-direction: column; justify-content: center; text-align: center;\">\n      <div style=\"font-weight: 700; font-size: 0.9rem;\">Shared model</div>\n      <div style=\"font-size: 0.7rem; font-family: var(--sl-font-mono); opacity: 0.7;\">tool-agnostic</div>\n    </div>\n    <div style=\"padding: 0.4rem 0;\">\n      <div style=\"font-weight: 600; font-size: 0.9rem;\">One <code>Conversation</code> type, shape-compatible with OpenAI Chat Completions</div>\n      <div style=\"font-size: 0.85rem; opacity: 0.8; margin-top: 0.2rem;\">Anthropic content-blocks preserved inside (<code>text</code> / <code>tool_use</code> / <code>tool_result</code> / <code>thinking</code>). Extensions bags at both conversation and message level carry tool-specific bits without polluting the core types.</div>\n    </div>\n  </div>\n  <div style=\"display: grid; grid-template-columns: 8rem 1fr; gap: 0.75rem; align-items: stretch;\">\n    <div style=\"background: var(--sl-color-purple-low); border: 2px solid var(--sl-color-purple); border-radius: 10px; padding: 0.5rem 0.75rem; display: flex; flex-direction: column; justify-content: center; text-align: center;\">\n      <div style=\"font-weight: 700; font-size: 0.9rem;\">Renderer + transforms</div>\n      <div style=\"font-size: 0.7rem; font-family: var(--sl-font-mono); opacity: 0.7;\">output shape</div>\n    </div>\n    <div style=\"padding: 0.4rem 0;\">\n      <div style=\"font-weight: 600; font-size: 0.9rem;\">Format and optionally rewrite on the way out</div>\n      <div style=\"font-size: 0.85rem; opacity: 0.8; margin-top: 0.2rem;\"><code>markdown</code> for humans and agents, <code>json</code> for machines. Path-rewrite transforms (<code>wsl-to-win</code>, <code>win-to-wsl</code>, <code>strip</code>) are opt-in and apply to content only — <code>cwd</code> metadata stays verbatim.</div>\n    </div>\n  </div>\n</div>\n\n## The `Conversation` shape\n\n<div style=\"background: var(--sl-color-gray-6); border-radius: 10px; padding: 1rem; margin: 1.5rem 0; font-family: var(--sl-font-mono); font-size: 0.85rem;\">\n<pre style=\"margin: 0;\"><code>{`Conversation {\n  id,                // session UUID\n  title?,            // derived from first user message\n  cwd?,              // launch-time working dir\n  started_at?,\n  messages: [\n    Message {\n      role,          // user | assistant | system | tool\n      content: [\n        Text { text } |\n        ToolUse { id, name, input } |\n        ToolResult { tool_use_id, output, is_error } |\n        Thinking { text } |\n        Unknown { raw }        ← resilience hook\n      ],\n      timestamp?,\n      extensions,    // adapter-specific per-message bits\n    }\n  ],\n  extensions,        // adapter-specific per-conversation bits\n                     //   - system_events (dropped from messages)\n                     //   - unknown_records (safety net)\n}`}</code></pre>\n</div>\n\n<Aside type=\"note\" title=\"Why extensions bags\">\nEvery tool we'll ever adapt has fields the core schema doesn't promote (Claude Code has <code>gitBranch</code>, <code>permissionMode</code>, <code>thinkingMetadata</code>, <code>isCompactSummary</code>, …). Flattening them into the core pollutes the model; dropping them loses data. A <code>serde_json::Value</code> extensions bag at both levels is the third option — tool-specific bits survive the round trip without the core types having to know about them.\n</Aside>\n\n## What the adapter classifies\n\nThe Claude Code adapter encounters six top-level record types in\npractice plus five more surfaced in production after the initial\nspike. Each falls into one of three buckets:\n\n<div style=\"display: grid; grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr 1fr; gap: 0.75rem; margin: 1.5rem 0;\">\n  <div style=\"border: 2px solid var(--sl-color-green); border-radius: 10px; padding: 0.75rem; background: var(--sl-color-green-low);\">\n    <div style=\"font-weight: 700; color: var(--sl-color-green-high); margin-bottom: 0.4rem;\">Schema</div>\n    <div style=\"font-size: 0.8rem; opacity: 0.85; margin-bottom: 0.4rem;\">Normalized into <code>messages</code>.</div>\n    <div style=\"font-family: var(--sl-font-mono); font-size: 0.75rem;\">\n      <code>user</code><br/>\n      <code>assistant</code>\n    </div>\n  </div>\n  <div style=\"border: 2px solid var(--sl-color-orange); border-radius: 10px; padding: 0.75rem; background: var(--sl-color-orange-low);\">\n    <div style=\"font-weight: 700; color: var(--sl-color-orange-high); margin-bottom: 0.4rem;\">Extensions</div>\n    <div style=\"font-size: 0.8rem; opacity: 0.85; margin-bottom: 0.4rem;\">Preserved in <code>extensions</code>, not rendered.</div>\n    <div style=\"font-family: var(--sl-font-mono); font-size: 0.75rem;\">\n      <code>system</code> → <code>system_events</code><br/>\n      <code>permission-mode</code><br/>\n      <code>attachment</code><br/>\n      <code>custom-title</code><br/>\n      <code>agent-name</code><br/>\n      <em>(unknowns)</em>\n    </div>\n  </div>\n  <div style=\"border: 2px solid var(--sl-color-gray-4); border-radius: 10px; padding: 0.75rem; background: var(--sl-color-gray-6);\">\n    <div style=\"font-weight: 700; margin-bottom: 0.4rem;\">Skipped</div>\n    <div style=\"font-size: 0.8rem; opacity: 0.85; margin-bottom: 0.4rem;\">Dropped — not load-bearing for paste workflows.</div>\n    <div style=\"font-family: var(--sl-font-mono); font-size: 0.75rem;\">\n      <code>file-history-snapshot</code><br/>\n      <code>progress</code><br/>\n      <code>queue-operation</code><br/>\n      <code>last-prompt</code>\n    </div>\n  </div>\n</div>\n\nThe full per-record contract is in the\n[adapter notes](/portaconv/reference/adapter-claude-code/).\n\n## Subagent filter\n\nSubagent sessions are transient — they're called by a parent session's\ntool_use, do their work, and return a consolidated result. Listing\nthem alongside top-level sessions in <code>pconv list</code> is noise\nfor paste workflows, so the adapter filters them out. Two shapes exist:\n\n<div style=\"display: grid; grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr; gap: 0.75rem; margin: 1.5rem 0;\">\n  <div style=\"border: 1px solid var(--sl-color-gray-4); border-radius: 10px; padding: 0.75rem; background: var(--sl-color-gray-6);\">\n    <div style=\"font-weight: 600; font-size: 0.85rem; margin-bottom: 0.3rem;\">old shape <span style=\"font-weight: 400; opacity: 0.6; font-family: var(--sl-font-mono); font-size: 0.75rem;\">Claude ≤ 2.0.x</span></div>\n    <div style=\"font-family: var(--sl-font-mono); font-size: 0.75rem; opacity: 0.85;\">\n      &lt;project-dir&gt;/<br/>\n      &nbsp;&nbsp;agent-&lt;hash&gt;.jsonl\n    </div>\n  </div>\n  <div style=\"border: 1px solid var(--sl-color-gray-4); border-radius: 10px; padding: 0.75rem; background: var(--sl-color-gray-6);\">\n    <div style=\"font-weight: 600; font-size: 0.85rem; margin-bottom: 0.3rem;\">new shape <span style=\"font-weight: 400; opacity: 0.6; font-family: var(--sl-font-mono); font-size: 0.75rem;\">Claude ≥ 2.1.x</span></div>\n    <div style=\"font-family: var(--sl-font-mono); font-size: 0.75rem; opacity: 0.85;\">\n      &lt;project-dir&gt;/<br/>\n      &nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;parent-uuid&gt;/<br/>\n      &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;subagents/<br/>\n      &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;agent-*.jsonl\n    </div>\n  </div>\n</div>\n\n## Multi-session JSONLs\n\nA single on-disk JSONL can carry multiple sessionIds when Claude's\n<code>/compact</code> writes a continuation under a new session UUID\nbut appends to the same file. portaconv surfaces each distinct\nsessionId as its own <code>SessionMeta</code>, matching Claude's\nown <code>/resume</code> mental model where the sessionId — not the\nfile — is the identity.\n\n<Aside type=\"caution\" title=\"Tool-call state doesn't survive paste\">\nThe renderer preserves the tool-call intent (name + args) and the result body, but the paste lands in a fresh agent process with no running tools and no live file state. Re-runs happen against the current filesystem. For most recovery scenarios this is fine — the substantive reasoning is what carries over.\n</Aside>\n\n## Read-only, on-demand\n\nportaconv never writes to any tool's storage. There is no daemon,\nno file watcher, no auto-sync. Every <code>pconv</code> invocation\nreads the current state of disk and emits output. Simpler to reason\nabout, trivially reversible, composes with pipes.\n",
  "file_path": "/mnt/c/Users/Cybersader/Documents/1 Projects, Workspaces/portaconv/docs/src/content/docs/concepts/index.mdx"
}

Lands in a follow-up release once the rmcp vs community-crate choice is settled.\n:::\n\n## `pconv list`\n\nList conversations discoverable on this machine. Surfaces each\ndistinct sessionId — a single JSONL may hold several when `/compact`\nwrites a continuation to the same file.\n\n```sh\npconv list                          # table by default\npconv list --format json\npconv list --min-messages 5         # filter chatty-short placeholder sessions\n```\n\nOutput columns (table format): `session-id · msgs · updated · title`.\nTitle is derived from the first user message. Subagent JSONLs are\nfiltered by path pattern and do not appear in the list — see the\n[concepts page](/portaconv/concepts/#subagent-filter) for the rule.\n\n## `pconv dump <session-id>`\n\nRender one session to stdout. Markdown is the default (paste-ready);\nuse `--format json` for the raw normalized model.\n\n```sh\npconv dump 01234567-89ab-cdef-0123-456789abcdef\n\n# Markdown knobs\npconv dump <id> --include-thinking        # show assistant reasoning blocks\npconv dump <id> --full-results            # emit full tool-result bodies\npconv dump <id> --include-system-events   # append the system_events section\n\n# Path rewriting — content only, not cwd metadata\npconv dump <id> --rewrite wsl-to-win      # /mnt/c/… → C:\\…\npconv dump <id> --rewrite win-to-wsl      # C:\\… → /mnt/c/…\npconv dump <id> --rewrite strip           # replace absolute paths with <path>\n\n# Machine format\npconv dump <id> --format json\n```\n\n### Markdown output shape\n\nEach message becomes a heading (`## User` / `## Assistant`) followed by:\n\n- plain text (rendered verbatim)\n- tool calls as **tool call:** label + a fenced `json` block with pretty-printed input\n- tool results as **tool result:** label + a fenced code block (truncated to 600 chars by default; `--full-results` to expand)\n- thinking blocks hidden by default (`--include-thinking` to show)\n- unknown content blocks surface an HTML comment + inline note rather than silently dropping\n\n### Rewrite scope\n\n| Rewritten | Left alone |\n|---|---|\n| `ContentBlock::Text.text` (prose) | `Conversation.cwd` (authoring env metadata) |\n| `ContentBlock::ToolUse.input` (all strings inside the JSON, recursively) | `Message.extensions` (adapter-preserved raw bits) |\n| `ContentBlock::ToolResult.output` (result bodies) | `ContentBlock::ToolUse.id` / `tool_use_id` (opaque handles) |\n|  | `ContentBlock::Thinking.text` (internal reasoning) |\n\nWindows → WSL regex is bounded to avoid URL-scheme false positives\n(`https://` doesn't match `s://`). WSL → Windows only matches the\n`/mnt/<letter>/…` form, so bare Linux paths like `/home/alice/…`\nstay untouched.\n\n## `pconv mcp serve`\n\nPlanned stdio MCP server exposing:\n\n- **Tool** `list_conversations(since?, workspace_id?, limit?)`\n- **Tool** `get_conversation(id, format=\"markdown\"|\"json\", rewrite?)`\n- **Resource** template `convos://conversation/<id>`\n\nIntended `mcp.json` wiring when implemented:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"mcpServers\": {\n    \"portaconv\": {\n      \"command\": \"pconv\",\n      \"args\": [\"mcp\", \"serve\"]\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Non-goals for v0.1\n\n- No `pconv copy` (clipboard integration — v0.2). Pipe to `clip.exe` / `pbcopy` / `wl-copy` yourself.\n- No `pconv export --to <file>` (committable handoff docs — v0.2). Redirect stdout.\n- No search / FTS / embeddings — get-by-id only.\n- No writes back to any tool's storage. Ever. Read-only by design.",

- **Pipeline — JSONL → Adapter → Shared model → (opt-in) Transforms → Renderer → stdout**, rendered as a stacked-row diagram

- **Design principles** — 4-card grid for read-only / resilient / composable / future-accounting
- Callout clarifying what's NOT rewritten (cwd metadata, extensions)

win = 0; placeholder = 0\n    def walk(s):\n        return s.count('/mnt/'), s.count(chr(92)+chr(92)) + sum(1 for _ in range(len(s)-2) if s[_].isalpha() and s[_+1]==':' and s[_+2]==chr(92)), s.count('<path>')\n    for m in d['messages']:\n        for b in m.get('content', []):\n            if b.get('type') == 'text':\n                t = b.get('text','')\n                mnt += t.count('/mnt/')\n                # match X:\\\\ pattern (JSON-escaped backslash)\n                import re\n                win += len(re.findall(r'[A-Z]:\\\\\\\\', t))\n                placeholder += t.count('<path>')\n            elif b.get('type') == 'tool_use':\n                t = json.dumps(b.get('input', {}))\n                mnt += t.count('/mnt/')\n                import re\n                win += len(re.findall(r'[A-Z]:\\\\\\\\', t))\n                placeholder += t.count('<path>')\n            elif b.get('type') == 'tool_result':\n                t = b.get('output','')\n                mnt += t.count('/mnt/')\n                import re\n                win += len(re.findall(r'[A-Z]:\\\\\\\\', t))\n                placeholder += t.count('<path>')\n    cwd = d.get('cwd','(none)')\n    return mnt, win, placeholder, cwd\n\nfor label, path in [('none',      '/tmp/ptest-none.json'),\n                    ('wsl-to-win','/tmp/ptest-wsltowin.json'),\n                    ('strip',     '/tmp/ptest-strip.json')]:\n    mnt, win, ph, cwd = counts(path)\n    print(f'{label:>12}:  /mnt/={mnt:4}  X:\\\\\\\\={win:4}  <path>={ph:4}  cwd={cwd!r}')\n\"",

## Battery results

### ✅ Passes

| Test | Result |
|---|---|
| **Portagenty coexistence** | `pa list` recognizes portaconv workspace, 3 sessions parse, `id` UUID intact. No collision. |
| **Old session (v2.0.65, <proj-h>, 92 msgs)** | Loads cleanly. All 4 block types present. Zero `unknown_records` (predates the newer record types). All per-message extension fields (`gitBranch`, `isSidechain`, `parentUuid`, `userType`, `uuid`, `version`) populated 92/92. |
| **Compact-summary session (bff2f662, 642 msgs)** | 2 `isCompactSummary: true` markers surfaced as user-role messages, at indices 233 and 591. Preserved in `message.extensions`. |
| **Rewrite conservation (all 3 modes)** | Content: `/mnt/` 20 → 0 → 0 across none / wsl-to-win / strip. Target form appears exactly 20 times in the rewritten output. **cwd metadata untouched in all three** (as designed). |
| **Markdown structural** | 1167 lines, 92 `##` headings (matches msg count), 32 tool call + 32 tool result (balanced pairs), fence pairs even, 13 truncations (expected for long results), no suspicious escape corruption. |

### ⚠️ Found real correctness bug

**Multi-sessionId load is non-deterministic** when a sessionId lives in multiple physical files. Example: `1e8d07c1-…` lives in **4** files (its own 48MB file + 20MB sibling `782cd44a-…jsonl` via /compact continuation + Windows-encoded dup of both). Current `load()` returns on first match in walk order — which file wins is filesystem-order-dependent. Observed: got the 48MB file's 4395 messages, but a different run could have landed on the 20MB file's smaller slice.

The spike had predicted this as Phase 2 open question #1. I implemented option (a) — surface every distinct sessionId in `list()` — but `load()` doesn't complete the contract. It should either:
- **(b-pref)** Merge records matching the sessionId across all files containing it, OR
- **(c-pref)** Pick deterministically (largest file by count for that sessionId).

Flagging as `v0.2` blocker.

### ❌ Still not tested

- **Actual paste-resume.** Rendering markdown and structural-checking it ≠ pasting into a fresh Claude/opencode/claude.ai session and verifying the agent picks up context. That's a manual step.
- **Attachment / image blocks.** Haven't located a session carrying one. Unknown whether `ContentBlock::Unknown { raw }` passthrough survives the renderer.
- **Portagenty pa→pconv shim.** Doesn't exist yet by design (Phase 3).
- **Very-long sessions (8k+ msgs).** `list` surfaces them; `dump` hasn't been stress-tested.

### Recommendation

Open a `v0.2` tracking issue with:
1. Multi-file sessionId merge (the real bug)
2. WSL/Windows-encoded dir dedup (avoid listing same session twice)
3. Manual paste-resume verification checklist

Want me to log those as GitHub issues now while the context is fresh, or keep them as working notes?

## User

Log them in my repo or somewhere else?  explain the issue in a setence or two.  I thought the fundamental desing of portaconv should make it possible to avoid certain issues

## Assistant

## Assistant

You're right — I overstated "real bug". The pivot from sync→extract does handle this: each JSONL is a canonical source for the sessionId in its basename. Other occurrences are artifacts of path-poisoning duplication. The design-consistent fix is one line: **prefer the file whose basename stem matches the sessionId** (Claude's naming convention for a session's home file). Current `load()` returns on first walk order; polish, not blocker.

Logging 3 issues in your repo (cybersader/portaconv) — public, tracked alongside the code, closable via commit message when fixed.

## Assistant

**tool call:** `Bash`

```json
{
  "command": "gh issue create --repo cybersader/portaconv \\\n  --title \"pconv dump: prefer canonical home file when sessionId appears in multiple JSONLs\" \\\n  --label \"bug,v0.2\" \\\n  --body \"$(cat <<'EOF'\nA sessionId can live in multiple physical JSONLs: (1) its own home file `<uuid>.jsonl` in the WSL-encoded project dir, (2) the same file duplicated in the Windows-encoded sibling dir, and (3) occasional sibling files when `/compact` writes a continuation under a new sessionId but appends to the parent's file. Current `load()` returns on first walk-order match — non-deterministic.\n\n**Fix:** in `src/adapters/claude_code.rs::load`, prefer any candidate whose filename stem equals the requested sessionId (Claude's canonical home-file convention). Break ties by file size (larger = fuller history). Fall back to first walk-order match only when no basename-match exists. Aligns with portaconv's extract-don't-sync design — the canonical file is the source of truth; the other copies are path-poisoning artifacts, not data worth merging.\nEOF\n)\" 2>&1 | tail -3",
  "description": "Issue 1: load canonical home file preference"
}
```

## Assistant

**tool call:** `Bash`

```json
{
  "command": "gh issue create --repo cybersader/portaconv \\\n  --title \"pconv list: dedup same sessionId across WSL- and Windows-encoded dirs\" \\\n  --label \"enhancement,v0.2\" \\\n  --body \"$(cat <<'EOF'\nWhen a project has been launched from both WSL (`-mnt-c-…-proj/`) and Windows (`C--…-proj/`), the same sessionId appears twice in `list` with slightly-diverged message counts (e.g., 97d7b58b appeared with 8152 and 7983 msgs in my test corpus). Cosmetic noise, not a correctness bug, but confusing for users.\n\n**Fix:** dedup by sessionId in `ClaudeCode::list`, keeping the entry with the larger `message_count` (or the most recent `updated_at` on tie). Expose a `--show-duplicates` flag for users who explicitly want to see the divergent copies for manual reconciliation. Zero impact on `load()` once issue #1 is resolved — both work on the canonical file.\nEOF\n)\" 2>&1 | tail -3",
  "description": "Issue 2: list dedup WSL/Win"
}

## Assistant

**tool call:** `Bash`

```json
{
  "command": "gh issue create --repo cybersader/portaconv \\\n  --title \"pconv list: performance — ~50s on 2607-JSONL corpus\" \\\n  --label \"performance,v0.2\" \\\n  --body \"$(cat <<'EOF'\n`pconv list` walks every JSONL under `~/.claude/projects/` and line-scans each for `sessionId` / `cwd` / `timestamp` / `type`. Measured ~50s on a 2607-JSONL corpus (~5 GB on disk). Acceptable for one-off use, slow for shell completion / MCP list queries.\n\n**Fix:** persistent cache keyed by `(path, mtime, size)` under `$XDG_STATE_HOME/portaconv/`. Invalidate per-file when mtime changes. First run pays the full walk; subsequent runs only rescan files that changed. Design note: keep cache read-only-ish — portaconv reads on demand, so the cache is a convenience, not a source of truth. A missing or corrupt cache falls back to a full walk, doesn't error.\nEOF\n)\" 2>&1 | tail -3",
  "description": "Issue 3: list perf"
}
```

## Assistant

**tool call:** `Edit`

```json
{
  "file_path": "/mnt/c/Users/Cybersader/Documents/1 Projects, Workspaces/portaconv/src/adapters/claude_code.rs",
  "new_string": "    fn load(&self, id: &str) -> Result<Conversation> {\n        let root = projects_root().ok_or_else(|| anyhow!(\"no home dir\"))?;\n        // A sessionId can appear in multiple physical files: its home file,\n        // WSL/Windows-encoded duplicates, and sibling files when /compact\n        // writes a continuation under a new sessionId but appends to the\n        // parent's file. Prefer the canonical home file (basename stem ==\n        // sessionId); tie-break by size (larger = fuller history).\n        let mut candidates: Vec<PathBuf> = Vec::new();\n        for file in walk_jsonls(&root)? {\n            if is_subagent_file(&file) {\n                continue;\n            }\n            if file_contains_session(&file, id)? {\n                candidates.push(file);\n            }\n        }\n        if candidates.is_empty() {\n            return Err(anyhow!(\"session {id} not found under {}\", root.display()));\n        }\n        candidates.sort_by_key(|p| pick_rank(p, id));\n        parse_session(&candidates[0], id)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Lower rank = higher preference. Tuple ordering does the work:\n///   1. 0 if basename stem matches id, else 1 (home file wins)\n///   2. size in bytes, negated so larger wins on tie\nfn pick_rank(p: &Path, id: &str) -> (u8, i64) {\n    let stem = p.file_stem().and_then(|s| s.to_str()).unwrap_or(\"\");\n    let tier = if stem == id { 0 } else { 1 };\n    let size = std::fs::metadata(p).map(|m| m.len() as i64).unwrap_or(0);\n    (tier, -size)\n}",
  "old_string": "    fn load(&self, id: &str) -> Result<Conversation> {\n        let root = projects_root().ok_or_else(|| anyhow!(\"no home dir\"))?;\n        for file in walk_jsonls(&root)? {\n            if is_subagent_file(&file) {\n                continue;\n            }\n            if file_contains_session(&file, id)? {\n                return parse_session(&file, id);\n            }\n        }\n        Err(anyhow!(\"session {id} not found under {}\", root.display()))\n    }\n}",
  "replace_all": false
}

Same sessionId shows up multiple times when a project\n/// has been launched from both WSL and Windows — the two encoded-dir\n/// buckets each carry a copy. Callers that want the raw multi-entry\n/// view skip this step.\npub fn dedup_sessions(mut metas: Vec<SessionMeta>) -> Vec<SessionMeta> {\n    use std::collections::HashMap;\n    let mut best: HashMap<String, SessionMeta> = HashMap::new();\n    for m in metas.drain(..) {\n        match best.get(&m.id) {\n            Some(existing)\n                if (existing.message_count, existing.updated_at)\n                    >= (m.message_count, m.updated_at) => {}\n            _ => {\n                best.insert(m.id.clone(), m);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    let mut out: Vec<SessionMeta> = best.into_values().collect();\n    out.sort_by_key(|m| std::cmp::Reverse(m.updated_at));\n    out\n}",

  "new_string": "/// Resolve a --workspace-toml flag into a `WorkspaceScope` with the\n/// declared project paths populated. `None` → empty scope. Returns an\n/// error on `auto` if no TOML is found by walking up from cwd, or if\n/// the declared path doesn't exist or can't be parsed.\nfn build_workspace_scope(flag: Option<&str>) -> Result<WorkspaceScope> {\n    let Some(value) = flag else {\n        return Ok(WorkspaceScope::default());\n    };\n    let toml_path = if value == \"auto\" {\n        find_workspace_toml_upwards()?\n            .ok_or_else(|| anyhow!(\"no *.portagenty.toml found by walking up from cwd\"))?\n    } else {\n        std::path::PathBuf::from(value)\n    };\n    parse_workspace_toml(&toml_path)\n}\n\nfn find_workspace_toml_upwards() -> Result<Option<std::path::PathBuf>> {\n    let mut dir = std::env::current_dir()?;\n    loop {\n        for entry in std::fs::read_dir(&dir)?.flatten() {\n            let p = entry.path();\n            if !p.is_file() {\n                continue;\n            }\n            let name = p\n                .file_name()\n                .and_then(|n| n.to_str())\n                .unwrap_or_default();\n            // `*.portagenty.toml` (workspace file) — distinct from bare\n            // `portagenty.toml` (per-project file).\n            if name.ends_with(\".portagenty.toml\") && name != \".portagenty.toml\" {\n                return Ok(Some(p));\n            }\n        }\n        if !dir.pop() {\n            return Ok(None);\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn parse_workspace_toml(path: &std::path::Path) -> Result<WorkspaceScope> {\n    // Minimal parse — we only care about the `projects` array. std::path::PathBuf::from(\".\"));\n    let mut scope = WorkspaceScope::default();\n    // Projects default to the TOML file's own directory if no\n    // `projects = [...]` line is declared — same convention portagenty\n    // uses for a workspace with no explicit project list.\n    scope.project_paths.push(base.clone());\n    for line in body.lines() {\n        let line = line.trim();\n let expanded = expand_path(item, &base);\n            scope.project_paths.push(expanded);\n        }\n        break;\n    }\n    Ok(scope)\n}\n\nfn expand_path(input: &str, base: &std::path::Path) -> std::path::PathBuf {\n    let with_home = if let Some(rest) = input.strip_prefix('~') {\n        if let Some(home) = dirs::home_dir() {\n            home.join(rest.trim_start_matches('/'))\n        } else {\n            std::path::PathBuf::from(input)\n        }\n    } else {\n        std::path::PathBuf::from(input)\n    };\n    if with_home.is_absolute() {\n        with_home\n    } else {\n        base.join(with_home)\n    }\n}\n\npub fn run(cli: Cli) -> Result<()> {",

  "content": "//! Stdio MCP server.\n//!\n//! Minimal handcrafted JSON-RPC 2.0 implementation — no rmcp dependency.\n//! Stdio MCP is line-delimited JSON-RPC; each message is one JSON object\n//! on one line. We read lines from stdin, dispatch, write responses to\n//! stdout, and exit on EOF.\n//!\n//! Exposed surface (protocol version `2024-11-05`):\n//!\n//!   tools/\n//!     list_conversations     — lists sessions (workspace/since/min-messages)\n//!     get_conversation       — returns markdown or JSON for one session\n//!\n//!   resources/\n//!     convos://conversation/<id>   — read a session as markdown\n//!\n//! Errors follow JSON-RPC conventions (-32700 parse, -32600 invalid\n//! request, -32601 method not found, -32602 invalid params, -32603\n//! internal). Anything outside the known methods returns -32601 —\n//! MCP clients MUST treat that as \"not supported\" and carry on.\n\npub mod server;\n\npub use server::run_stdio_server;\n",
